## First Order

[Fascist](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism"),[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) [neo-Imperialist](/wiki/Neo-Imperialism "Neo-Imperialism")[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) military junta[[3]](#cite_note-Abrams_Luke_Skywalker-3)

## Other information

### Affiliation

* [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") (secretly)[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)
  + [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") (secretly)[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9)
  + [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order")[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Government)

:   "*The First Order is* not *the Empire. We are purer. We have been through the* crucible *and emerged* stronger*.*"  
    "*I agree, Phasma. The First Order is not the Empire. But perhaps, one day, if we all work very hard and do our very, very best… It could be.*"
:   ―Phasma and Terex[[17]](#cite_note-Poe_2-17)

The **First Order** ([21 ABY](/wiki/21_ABY "21 ABY")-[35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY")), or simply the **Order**, was a [fascist](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") [military junta](/wiki/First_Order_High_Command "First Order High Command") which dwelled in the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions") of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") during the [era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era") of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"). The First Order was ruled by a [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") from their [mobile](/wiki/Supremacy "Supremacy") [headquarters](/wiki/Steadfast_(Resurgent-class) "Steadfast (Resurgent-class)") instead of a traditional [planetary](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital"). A [militaristic](/wiki/Stratocracy "Stratocracy") [dictatorship](/wiki/Dictatorship "Dictatorship") that wished to remove disorder from existence and had a fanatical devotion to the totalitarian notions of [order](/wiki/Neo-Imperialism "Neo-Imperialism") and a disdain for [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy"). To this end, it became locked in a [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") with the New Republic and spreading influence from beyond the confines of unknown [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"), ending with the First Order [staging an invasion](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") of the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy"), but were repelled by the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") and [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), causing the First Order to [fall](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order").

After the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), publicly known as [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Sheev Palpatine, in the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") [fell](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") and broke into various [Imperial Remnants](/wiki/Imperial_Remnants "Imperial Remnants"). Spearheaded by [Counselor to the Empire](/wiki/Counselor_to_the_Empire "Counselor to the Empire") [Gallius Rax](/wiki/Gallius_Rax "Gallius Rax"), some of the [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military") retreated into the Unknown Regions, which the Empire had secretly charted in the past. After blazing through ancient [hyperspace trails](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"), retreating Imperials met secret reinforcements, where [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane") intended to build a stronger and purer Empire. In the [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after, Sloane's [remnant forces](/wiki/Unknown_Regions_Imperial_remnant "Unknown Regions Imperial remnant") formed the First Order that plotted a return to power and sought to reclaim lost [Imperial legacy](/wiki/New_Order "New Order").

Sloane and [Commandant](/wiki/Commandant "Commandant") [Brendol Hux](/wiki/Brendol_Hux "Brendol Hux") were among the first leaders of the First Order. The [fleets](/wiki/First_Order_Navy "First Order Navy") and [armies](/wiki/First_Order_Army "First Order Army") that they secretly built comprised a vast and technologically superior [military](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military") at the First Order's disposal. Through [Project Resurrection](/wiki/Project_Resurrection "Project Resurrection"), the First Order conscripted [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling")—thousands of whom were abducted from outlying [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system")—and trained them as the [new generation of stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper"). The First Order also undertook a major offensive to seize several hermetic kingdoms and their resources in the Unknown Regions. Eventually, the mysterious [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") rose to power as Supreme Leader, who was in fact an [artificial](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") [Strand-Cast](/wiki/Strand-Cast "Strand-Cast") that served as the proxy the [revived](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious from the hidden world of [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"). With its original leaders mostly sidelined, the First Order become subservient to the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") [cult](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult") that Sidious and his plans to use turn the First Order into a template for a resurgent [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire"). Much of the First Order, however, was unaware of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith")'s influence over their organization.

The First Order was publicly formed by the [Centrist](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists")-aligned [star](/wiki/Star "Star") systems that [seceded](/wiki/First_Order_secession "First Order secession") from the New Republic as a result of [instability](/wiki/Amaxine_warrior_crisis "Amaxine warrior crisis") in the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate"). Throughout the Cold War, the First Order and the New Republic existed in a state of tension with occasional skirmishes but no direct fighting. As the First Order became increasingly hostile toward the New Republic, former [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") founded the Resistance to monitor its activities. However, the Senate refused to take forceful [military](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Force "New Republic Defense Force") action against them, believing that they posed no credible threat. The First Order also began to search for [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), to prevent the rise of a new [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi").

In [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"), the galaxy fell into a state of [crisis](/wiki/Starkiller_crisis "Starkiller crisis") when the First Order fired its [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon"), [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base"), at the [Hosnian system](/wiki/Hosnian_system "Hosnian system"), completely [destroying](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm") the New Republic capital of [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"). Although the Resistance succeeded in destroying the weapon during the [Battle of Starkiller Base](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base"), they were unable to stop the First Order's invasion of the galaxy. During the [Battle of Oetchi](/wiki/Battle_of_Oetchi "Battle of Oetchi"), Snoke was [assassinated](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") by his apprentice, the [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), who usurped the title of Supreme Leader. The First Order conquered much of the known galaxy under Ren's leadership, which was met with defiance and rebellion, to which Ren responded by enforcing a heavily brutal suppression of dissent.

In [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"), Ren formed an alliance with Sidious after discovering the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order")—a massive [fleet](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet") of [*Xyston*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Xyston-class_Star_Destroyer "Xyston-class Star Destroyer") built by the Sith Eternal—on Exegol. Sidious promised Ren control of his [forces](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_military "Sith Eternal military") and the chance to succeed him as Galactic [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") if he [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") the [Jedi apprentice](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"). However, Ren's ambition to rule the First Order as a true Empire ended when he [renounced](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") and returned to the [light side](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") as Ben Solo. Despite the loss of the Supreme Leader, [Allegiant General](/wiki/Allegiant_General "Allegiant General") [Enric Pryde](/wiki/Enric_Pryde "Enric Pryde") swore his allegiance to Sidious, who declared himself Emperor once more. However, his plans for the Sith resurrection were thwarted by Rey and Ben Solo during the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol"), where the Emperor was ultimately destroyed along with his [followers](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist"). Without the support of Sith reinforcements, the First Order failed to quell the uprising against its rule and ultimately collapsed in the wake of the Resistance's victory at Exegol, even though an entire generation consisting of countless officers and stormtroopers remained along with missing foundries and hubs of manufacturing unaccounted for.

## History[]

### Rise and fall of Empire[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and [Contingency](/wiki/Contingency "Contingency")

:   "*Palpatine felt that the universe beyond the edges of our maps was where his power came from. Over the many years he, with our aid, sent men and women beyond known space. They built labs and communication stations on distant moons, asteroids, out there in the wilds. We must follow them. Retreat from the galaxy. Go out beyond the veil of stars.*"
:   ―Yupe Tashu[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

 [![The Emperor posthumously triggered the Contingency which decreed the destruction of the Galactic Empire for failing to protect him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/SidEmp.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008110258) [![The Emperor posthumously triggered the Contingency which decreed the destruction of the Galactic Empire for failing to protect him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/SidEmp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20201008110258)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/SidEmp.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008110258) 

The Emperor posthumously triggered the Contingency which decreed the destruction of the Galactic Empire for failing to protect him.

 

For roughly a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"), the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") maintained peace and stability within [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), aided by the efforts of the monastic [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and the [Judicial Forces](/wiki/Judicial_Forces "Judicial Forces"). With the believed extinction of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith")—ancient enemies of the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and the Republic—the ruling [Dark Lord](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") secretly plotted to overthrow the Republic with the formation of his own [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire").[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_I-19)[[20]](#cite_note-Episode_II-20) Sidious, along with his [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Darth Tyranus](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), orchestrated the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") by fomenting political chaos across the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy"). Through his apprentice, Sidious secretly commanded a rival galactic government known as the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") throughout the destructive three-[year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") [period](/wiki/Time "Time") that was the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), while he remained the [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") of the Republic as Sheev Palpatine long beyond the expiration of his term. Gradually amassing far more emergency powers than would be ordinarily allowed through the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), along with radically amending the [Galactic Constitution](/wiki/Galactic_Constitution "Galactic Constitution"), Sidious eventually oversaw the [destruction](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") of the Jedi Order and the [defeat](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") of the Separatists through his new apprentice, [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"). Sidious, as Chancellor Palpatine, then issued the [proclamation of the New Order](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order"),[[21]](#cite_note-Tarkin-21) officially transforming the thousand-year-old [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") and installing himself as the first [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") with the support of the Senate.[[22]](#cite_note-Episode_III-22)

With the [purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the Jedi and a massive military to enforce his will, Sidious remained largely unchallenged as [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") throughout the initial nineteen years of his [reign](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), embarking on a gradual conquest of the galaxy. Eventually, the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") was formed to oppose his aggressive expansion and genocidal actions,[[23]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-23) resulting in the outbreak of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War")[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-24) that spanned years of [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history").[[25]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-25) Four years after the [destruction](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin") of the [first Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") by [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"),[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-24) the Empire suffered a decisive defeat at the Battle of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"), where the more powerful [Death Star II](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") was destroyed, and along with it, the Emperor and his apprentice, [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader.[[26]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-26)

 [![One of Palpatine closest advisers, Yupe Tashu, suggested that the Empire retreat into the Unknown Regions, which had been seeded with shipyards, laboratories, and storehouses.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/YupeTashu-BattleOfJakkuInsurgencyRising2.png/revision/latest?cb=20241017144057) [![One of Palpatine closest advisers, Yupe Tashu, suggested that the Empire retreat into the Unknown Regions, which had been seeded with shipyards, laboratories, and storehouses.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/YupeTashu-BattleOfJakkuInsurgencyRising2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241017144057)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/YupeTashu-BattleOfJakkuInsurgencyRising2.png/revision/latest?cb=20241017144057) 

One of Palpatine closest advisers, Yupe Tashu, suggested that the Empire retreat into the Unknown Regions, which had been seeded with shipyards, laboratories, and storehouses.

 

Unknown to anyone but a select few, however, the Emperor had long been sending Imperial [scouts](/wiki/Scout "Scout") and other constructive efforts to the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions") of [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"),[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) with assistance from a collection of high-ranking power players within the Empire, including his [advisor](/wiki/Emperor%27s_adviser "Emperor's adviser") [Yupe Tashu](/wiki/Yupe_Tashu "Yupe Tashu") and the individuals that went on to form the [Imperial Future Council](/wiki/Imperial_Future_Council "Imperial Future Council").[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18) Over the course of decades, the Unknown Regions had been seeded with shipyards, laboratories, and storehouses that would serve to prepare for the Empire's rebirth as part of Sidious' [Contingency](/wiki/Contingency "Contingency") in the rare event of his [death](/wiki/Death "Death").[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) His plan was to ensure the Galactic Empire's destruction as he believed that an Empire should not outlive its Emperor[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) and its' inability to defend him made it unworthy of continued existence.[[29]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-29) However, he also planned the creation of a new Empire beyond the borders of known space; resources and select personnel were discreetly funnelled to the Unknown Regions, where the Empire could begin anew.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) Per Sidious's plans, only the most ruthless of Imperial personnel would remain to forge the new state.[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) Sidious entrusted the task of executing the Contingency to his protégé, [Gallius Rax](/wiki/Gallius_Rax "Gallius Rax").[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28)

Following another year of bloody conflict, the fractured Empire made its last stand over the sandy wastes of [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), which had become a rallying point for retreating Imperials, against the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), resulting in many casualties on both sides of the conflict[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) as part of the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku").[[30]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-30)
On Jakku, a secret Imperial research base,[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) the [Jakku Observatory](/wiki/Jakku_Observatory "Jakku Observatory"), housed ancient [computers](/wiki/Computer "Computer") which plotted out computerized routes through the Unknown Regions. These computers used information derived from [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo"),[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) who hailed from the [Chiss Ascendancy](/wiki/Chiss_Ascendancy "Chiss Ascendancy"),[[31]](#cite_note-Thrawn-31) and the survey teams and [probe droids](/wiki/Probe_droid "Probe droid") that the Emperor had previously sent to explore these routes.[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) Jakku came to serve as a jumping-off point for Imperial [warships](/wiki/Warship "Warship") heading into the Unknown Regions,[[32]](#cite_note-Jakku_DB-32) and the retreating Imperials destroyed the research base before the New Republic could reach it.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

 [![Gallius Rax, the Emperor's protégé, spearheaded efforts for the exodus into the Unknown Regions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/GalliusRexVariantClear-RUS-4.png/revision/latest?cb=20250310103316) [![Gallius Rax, the Emperor's protégé, spearheaded efforts for the exodus into the Unknown Regions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/GalliusRexVariantClear-RUS-4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20250310103316)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/GalliusRexVariantClear-RUS-4.png/revision/latest?cb=20250310103316) 

Gallius Rax, the Emperor's protégé, spearheaded efforts for the exodus into the Unknown Regions.

 

As part of the Contingency, Rax's secret objective in the Battle of Jakku was to destroy the planet to cripple both the remnants of the Empire and the New Republic; however, he was prevented from carrying out this phase by Grand [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane"), who killed Rax. In his dying words, Rax urged Sloane to take his place in the Contingency with [Commandant](/wiki/Commandant "Commandant") [Brendol Hux](/wiki/Brendol_Hux "Brendol Hux"), his son [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux"), and their [child soldiers](/wiki/Gallius_Rax%27s_child_soldiers "Gallius Rax's child soldiers") aboard the [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") [*Imperialis*](/wiki/Imperialis_(Jakku) "Imperialis (Jakku)") and rendezvous with the Emperor's flagship, the [Super Star Destroyer](/wiki/Super_Star_Destroyer "Super Star Destroyer") [*Eclipse*](/wiki/Eclipse_(Executor-class) "Eclipse (Executor-class)"), which had been dispatched in advance to the Unknown Regions. Their journey took several months and consisted of many short [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace") jumps, during which time Sloane discovered that the *Imperialis* had been transmitting coordinates to other Imperial [fleets](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet"). Upon regrouping with the *Eclipse*, Sloane ordered the [Sentinel](/wiki/Sentinel_(Contingency) "Sentinel (Contingency)") piloting the *Imperialis* to bring the ship in and rejoin with the others. There, she intended to board and saw an opportunity to rebuild the Empire; one that was stronger and purer, and not given to the backstabbing and incest of the Galactic Empire.[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28)

Defeated at Jakku and facing severe internal unrest, the Empire was forced to sign the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance"), severely limiting its ability to wage war and ushering in its demise[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) Imperial [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda") and New Republic [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)") [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma") signed the Galactic Concordance, which called for the dissolution of the Galactic Empire. Chancellor Mothma then issued another declaration designating all surviving [Imperial officers](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") as war criminals,[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) while the Empire began to break into remnants. A [remnant](/wiki/Inner_systems%27_Imperial_remnant "Inner systems' Imperial remnant") of Imperial vessels was confined to predetermined boundaries by the New Republic in the [Core](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") and [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories")[[30]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-30) while a [provisional government](/wiki/Coruscant%27s_provisional_government "Coruscant's provisional government") led by Amedda was established on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), the former [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of the Old Republic[[19]](#cite_note-Episode_I-19) and [throneworld](/wiki/Throneworld "Throneworld") of the Empire, where it was overseen by Republic observers.[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28)

After the signing of the Galactic Concordance, the New Republic arrived in systems still under Imperial control to announce the signing of the historic peace treaty. However, by the time the Republic reached these systems, fleets had already retreated to the Unknown Regions. The battle's end at Jakku was marked by the sudden departure of the surviving Imperial warships into the Unknown Regions following the announcement of the treaty, where they had seemingly disappeared.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) During the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era"), multiple [Imperial Remnants](/wiki/Imperial_Remnants "Imperial Remnants") were represented on the [Shadow Council](/wiki/Shadow_Council_(Imperial_Remnants) "Shadow Council (Imperial Remnants)"), allowing them to coordinate efforts that subvert the New Republic.[[33]](#cite_note-Chapter_23-33) The [original Council](/wiki/Shadow_Council "Shadow Council") was created by Rax[[34]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-34) prior to his death on Jakku.[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28)

### Early foundations[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Unknown Regions Imperial remnant](/wiki/Unknown_Regions_Imperial_remnant "Unknown Regions Imperial remnant")

:   "*But what we can ascertain is that, for a period at least, the organisation and administration of what would become the First Order was based on military lines, and that it was likely the recipient of a great deal of covert financial support from the Corporate Sector Authority.*"
:   ―Beaumont Kin, *The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire*[[35]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-35)

 [![While in hiding in the Unknown Regions, the organisation of what would become the First Order was formed under Sloane's direction](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/AdmiralSloane-BTCG.png/revision/latest?cb=20211113002413) [![While in hiding in the Unknown Regions, the organisation of what would become the First Order was formed under Sloane's direction](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/AdmiralSloane-BTCG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211113002413)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/AdmiralSloane-BTCG.png/revision/latest?cb=20211113002413) 

While in hiding in the Unknown Regions, the organisation of what would become the First Order was formed under Sloane's direction

 

In an effort to escape the prying eyes of the New Republic and restore the Empire after the Battle of Jakku,[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) a major [remnant](/wiki/Unknown_Regions_Imperial_remnant "Unknown Regions Imperial remnant") of warships,[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) [officers](/wiki/Officer "Officer"), [nobles](/wiki/Noble "Noble"), [technologists](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist"),[[36]](#cite_note-FO_Databank-36) and [warlords](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord")[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) fled the known galaxy[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) as part of an exodus[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) into the Unknown Regions spearheaded by Rax, Sloane, and Hux.[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) Beyond the *Imperialis*'s signal to Imperial fleets,[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) the Imperials were also guided into uncharted space thanks to the dark side adept known as [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"), whose [Attendants](/wiki/Attendants "Attendants") had access to ancient [hyperspace routes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route") the Imperials likely would have died without.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) All the same, the Imperial remnant blazed across the badly mapped star systems of the Unknown Regions over the course of years. Eventually, however, they found a foothold on planets the Empire had secretly charted in the past.[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) Within the Unknown Regions, they met secret reinforcements[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) and plotted a return to power, for which they began to build fleets and [armies](/wiki/Army "Army") in secret to reclaim the Imperial legacy.[[36]](#cite_note-FO_Databank-36) By [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[37]](#cite_note-MandoDate-37) Brendol Hux represented his remnant in the [Shadow Council](/wiki/Shadow_Council_(Imperial_Remnants) "Shadow Council (Imperial Remnants)"), overseeing affairs related to [Project Necromancer](/wiki/Project_Necromancer "Project Necromancer"),[[33]](#cite_note-Chapter_23-33) a [cloning](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") operation that had been of great interest to the late Emperor during early years of his reign.[[38]](#cite_note-The_Cavalry_Has_Arrived-38) Meanwhile, the Imperial remnant in the galaxy proper[[28]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-28) withered away into a remnant of political hardliners locked in a cold war with the New Republic until they reformed into[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) what became[[36]](#cite_note-FO_Databank-36) the mysterious First Order[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) that started in the Unknown Regions.[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2)

The emerging[[39]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-39) First Order began kidnapping children to fill out the ranks of its new [military](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military"),[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) specifically targeting the children of former Rebel leaders. Amongst those taken was the daughter of Rebel General [Landonis Balthazar Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian"),[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-4) [Kadara](/wiki/Kadara_Calrissian "Kadara Calrissian"), who was kidnapped in [15 ABY](/wiki/15_ABY "15 ABY"). All the same, in [21 ABY](/wiki/21_ABY "21 ABY"),[[40]](#cite_note-21_ABY_Date-40) the [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military") sat in tatters and had fled across the galaxy's farthest reaches,[[41]](#cite_note-211_Launchpad-41) with even the Imperial hideouts of the Unknown Regions remaining scattered. Still,[[39]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-39) those hidden[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) Unknown Regions Imperial holdouts[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) started to form a new chain of command, albeit an obscure and skeletal one, for Imperial survivors. Amongst their followers was [Enric Pryde](/wiki/Enric_Pryde "Enric Pryde"), who was ordered to establish ties with the [Corporate Sector Authority](/wiki/Corporate_Sector_Authority "Corporate Sector Authority"). The Sith Eternal secretly trusted Pryde as a valuable follower and thus dispatched [Ochi of Bestoon](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi") to meet with him during the [assassin's mission](/wiki/Quest_for_Exegol "Quest for Exegol") for the Emperor.[[39]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-39) Later in 21 ABY, the First Order was founded[[15]](#cite_note-Timelines-15) by the Unknown Regions remnant, who regrouped themselves[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) from once scattered hideouts[[39]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-39) into the First Order.[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2)[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) Indeed, the rise of the First Order entailed festering Imperial remnants uniting and blooming into that singular, new force.[[42]](#cite_note-231History-42)

 [![Brendol Hux, a founder of the First Order, was a predominant figure in the early First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/BrendolHuxMando.png/revision/latest?cb=20230412083322) [![Brendol Hux, a founder of the First Order, was a predominant figure in the early First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/BrendolHuxMando.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230412083322)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/BrendolHuxMando.png/revision/latest?cb=20230412083322) 

Brendol Hux, a founder of the First Order, was a predominant figure in the early First Order.

 

The First Order specifically grew from the [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics"), military, and spiritual[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) elements of the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order"),[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) with Sloane and Hux becoming part of its first set of leaders.[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) A military junta[[3]](#cite_note-Abrams_Luke_Skywalker-3) influenced by the principles of the fallen Empire,[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43) the origins of the First Order thus dated back to the Galactic Empire, with the remnants of the Imperial Military forming the basis of the [First Order military](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military"). The [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") was the First Order's secretive spiritual branch;[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) as a [Sith cult](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult"), they preserved the Sith [religion](/wiki/Religion "Religion") and revered the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") from their base of operations on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"). Additionally, the Sith Eternal [cultists](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist") were dedicated to building a new [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire"), secretly working to ensure the First Order's conquest of the galaxy.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) The rise of the First Order took advantage of the New Republic's failure to properly exert its authority or truly patrol the Outer Rim.[[44]](#cite_note-217_End-44) Beyond that, the First Order would keep its emerging military might hidden within the Unknown Regions, where they avoided the eyes of the New Republic. The [First Order Navy](/wiki/First_Order_Navy "First Order Navy")'s ideology would be focused on mobility and individual firepower due to its much smaller fleet in comparison to the Old Empire.[[45]](#cite_note-POV_220-45) As an entity that claimed the mantle of a successor to the fallen Empire, the elite of the First Order included within its numbers the members of the wealthy dynasties that had once belonged to the Imperial aristocracy during Palpatine’s reign. Having maintained their devotion to the Imperial vision for building a better galactic order that was formed through any means necessary, these lineages — including the [Jerjerrod family](/wiki/Jerjerrod_family "Jerjerrod family") — were counted among the upper class of the First Order and commanded respect from various members.[[46]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Vodran-46)

### The rise of Snoke[]

:   "*Through my manipulation of Snoke, I began gathering forces, building an army capable of opposing the New Republic that had arisen in my absence. Through Snoke, I would make certain that the First Order would be mine to control.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[29]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-29)

 [![The First Order fell under the control of Supreme Leader Snoke, a strandcast created by Darth Sidious to control the First Order and make it a force capable of opposing the New Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Snoke-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250125025401) [![The First Order fell under the control of Supreme Leader Snoke, a strandcast created by Darth Sidious to control the First Order and make it a force capable of opposing the New Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Snoke-CGSWG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250125025401)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Snoke-CGSWG.png/revision/latest?cb=20250125025401) 

The First Order fell under the control of Supreme Leader Snoke, a strandcast created by Darth Sidious to control the First Order and make it a force capable of opposing the New Republic.

 

Just as many of the Emperor's servants carried the Old Empire's greatest military secrets to the Unknown Regions, so too did Snoke, who eventually rose to become[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) the [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") of the First Order.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) Had it not been for the ancient [hyperspace trails](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route") blazed through the Unknown Regions by Snoke's [Attendants](/wiki/Attendants "Attendants"), most of the former Imperial officers would have likely perished crossing into the uncharted realm.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) Snoke was a mysterious humanoid, with very scant details as to regarding his origins,[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) strong with the dark side of the Force.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) Despite his abilities not being explicitly Sith in origin, Snoke's powerful abilities as a force user and knowledge made him the undisputed heir as the leader to the forces gathered under the Contingency.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

Snoke was, in fact, one of the many [artificial](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") [strandcasts](/wiki/Strand-Cast "Strand-Cast") [created](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") by the Emperor and his cult following, the Sith Eternal, prior to his demise, and discarded as a potential vessel for the Sith Lord's dark essence.[[29]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-29) Instead, Snoke was made to serve as a proxy ruler for his creator and influenced by the zombified Sith Lord from afar[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) to gather the forces that would go to make the armies of the First Order and spread his influence across the galaxy through less direct means. With that, Sidious ensured that the new empire which arose after the Battle of Jakku was his to control.[[29]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-29) The First Order did not know of Snoke's origins, though some came to peer behind the veil of secrecy and realized that he was subservient to some unseen force.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) Snoke himself was possibly unaware of the factual nature surrounding his existence,[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) and indeed remained unaware of his status as a pawn in Sidious's larger game for his entire life.[[47]](#cite_note-Snoke_&_Mirrors:_Emperor_Palpatine's_Top_5_Proxies-47)

 [![Darth Sidious secretly manipulated the First Order from the shadows, intending to absorb the junta into the new Sith Empire his followers were building.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Insider197-Palpatineresurrected.png/revision/latest?cb=20231024055024) [![Darth Sidious secretly manipulated the First Order from the shadows, intending to absorb the junta into the new Sith Empire his followers were building.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Insider197-Palpatineresurrected.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231024055024)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c9/Insider197-Palpatineresurrected.png/revision/latest?cb=20231024055024) 

Darth Sidious secretly manipulated the First Order from the shadows, intending to absorb the junta into the new Sith Empire his followers were building.

 

The Emperor's resurrection, the existence of his followers, the Sith Eternal, and their hidden base of operations, Exegol, were all secrets unknown to even the highest echelons of the First Order. Much of the First Order was even unaware of the Contingency itself nor their ultimate purpose in it, for as the First Order served as its military wing, the Sith Eternal lay at its spiritual heart. The true leadership of the First Order operated from behind a veil of secrecy, driven by the tenets of the dark side of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") and the ancient ways of the Sith.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) From afar, the phantom Emperor, working from the shadows,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) forged the remnants of the Empire into the First Order as he plotted his return to power.[[48]](#cite_note-Sidious_Bio_Gallery-48) Once the time was right, Sidious would return at the head of a new Sith Empire, which would absorb the First Order and sweep aside any other pretenders or states to control the galaxy.[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2)

Snoke's choices when governing the faction only added to his mysterious nature. The dark side adept made no designs toward the old title Emperor, relied on mysticism and focusing on spiritual matters while allowing his generals to wield the First Order military in his name, and was unwilling to meet in person with his subordinates, instead relying on large casting presence holograms to communicate with and to administer orders to the underlings who served him.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) Gallius Rax, Rae Sloane, [Ormes Apolin](/wiki/Ormes_Apolin "Ormes Apolin"), and Brendol Hux were originally seen as potential leaders of the Empire's remnants by the admirals and [generals](/wiki/General "General") who had survived the implosion of the Empire and the New Republic's wrath, but they were sidelined, co-opted, or destroyed by Snoke. Brendol's son, General Armitage Hux, was spared in the long term by Snoke in order to use him as a political tool in his rise to power.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) Pryde was eventually made privy to Palpatine's survival and became the Emperor's contact within the regime. In addition to Pryde, many of the young generation that the Sith Eternal harvested for [their army](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_army "Sith Eternal army") were originally conscripted into the First Order as children, but, due to their potential, spies culled and "disappeared" them, allowing them to become the [red](/wiki/Color "Color")-[armored](/wiki/Sith_trooper_armor "Sith trooper armor") [Sith troopers](/wiki/Sith_trooper "Sith trooper") that comprised the infantry of Darth Sidious' [new forces](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_military "Sith Eternal military").[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-4)

### New leaders[]

:   "*Someone in your army tried to kill you. Clearly, you've managed to inspire a lot of loyalty, Hux.*"  
    "*Oh, please. I thought you could read minds, Ren. You honestly believe people hate* me *more than they hate* you*?*"
:   ―Kylo Ren and Armitage Hux[[49]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance-49)

 [![Kylo Ren, General Armitage Hux, and Captain Phasma were members of a new generation of First Order leaders.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Phasma_Hux_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20170908043445) [![Kylo Ren, General Armitage Hux, and Captain Phasma were members of a new generation of First Order leaders.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Phasma_Hux_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170908043445)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Phasma_Hux_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20170908043445) 

Kylo Ren, General Armitage Hux, and Captain Phasma were members of a new generation of First Order leaders.

 

As the son of a founding member of the First Order, [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux") was raised in the organization's military wing[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) which [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Phasma](/wiki/Phasma "Phasma") joined after leaving her homeworld of [Parnassos](/wiki/Parnassos "Parnassos") with Brendol.[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5) Following the [Destruction of the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple"), former [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") joined the First Order under the persona of Kylo Ren. He became the [master](/wiki/Ren "Ren") of the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren") as well as the apprentice of Supreme Leader Snoke. Hailing from the powerful bloodline of the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family"), Ren had in his master's estimation the potential to become as strong as his grandfather Darth Vader.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) Unlike Armitage and Phasma, Ren did not possess an official rank in the First Order military. Nonetheless, as Snoke's apprentice he wielded the authority to command his master's forces.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

Ren, Armitage, and Phasma represented a new generation of leaders that supplanted the old guard in the First Order's command structure.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) As part of this turnover, Armitage and Phasma conspired to assassinate Brendol; Armitage had been abused by his father from his youth, while Phasma sought to erase her past. Armitage left the actual murder up to Phasma with his only instruction being to make it untraceable. Phasma carried out the killing of Brendol using the toxin from the bite of a [Parnassos beetle](/wiki/Parnassos_beetle "Parnassos beetle"). Armitage then gave a brief address to Captain [Cardinal](/wiki/Archex "Archex") and the [Stormtrooper Corps](/wiki/Stormtrooper_Corps_(First_Order) "Stormtrooper Corps (First Order)") informing them of Brendol's passing and ascended to his leadership role in the military, taking over from his late father.[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5)

At some point, a cargo ship was ambushed containing military gear which the ship's crew claimed was meant for the First Order. Among the possessions seized was a set of [stormtrooper armor](/wiki/Stormtrooper_armor "Stormtrooper armor") which was later presented to [Terex](/wiki/Terex "Terex"), a former [Imperial stormtrooper](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper") and, at the time, a crime lord of the [Ranc Gang](/wiki/Ranc_Gang "Ranc Gang"). Terex immediately became curious about the modern design and confirmed that it was not of Imperial design. After Terex asked of its origin, he continued to think about the implications of this new information. Sometime later, he subsequently joined the ranks of the [First Order Security Bureau](/wiki/First_Order_Security_Bureau "First Order Security Bureau").[[50]](#cite_note-Poe_10-50)

Meanwhile, the First Order had to contend with several threats that lurked within the Unknown Regions: hermetic kingdoms which were confronted by the Order. On Supreme Leader Snoke's instruction, the new military undertook a major offensive against several of these kingdoms to seize their worlds and resources to fuel their rise.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) Phasma herself led from the front as the First Order charted through the wilderness of the Unknown Regions,[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) while [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Frantis Griss](/wiki/Frantis_Griss "Frantis Griss") found himself gaining valuable experience from the expansion.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

### Cold War[]

#### The First Order emerges[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Amaxine warrior crisis](/wiki/Amaxine_warrior_crisis "Amaxine warrior crisis") and [First Order secession](/wiki/First_Order_secession "First Order secession")

:   "*Over time, the former Imperials reunited as the First Order and coolly inhabited a wing of Republic politics until tensions reached a breaking point. The First Order seceded from the New Republic, a move that was welcomed by many in the galactic capital. But others realized that without Republic oversight, the First Order would return to the Empire's draconian ways and ambitious expansion.*"
:   ―Janyor[[14]](#cite_note-Propaganda-14)

 [![The Amaxine warriors were a paramilitary group with secret ties to the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/Amaxine_Warriors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181104024622) [![The Amaxine warriors were a paramilitary group with secret ties to the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/Amaxine_Warriors.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181104024622)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d8/Amaxine_Warriors.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181104024622) 

The Amaxine warriors were a paramilitary group with secret ties to the First Order.

 

The First Order sought to weaken the New Republic and to generate funding to build up the [new navy](/wiki/First_Order_Navy "First Order Navy"). The First Order had used a militia group called the [Amaxine warriors](/wiki/Amaxine_warriors_(New_Republic_Era) "Amaxine warriors (New Republic Era)") as proxies to fund the [Nikto](/wiki/Nikto "Nikto") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Rinnrivin Di](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di "Rinnrivin Di")'s [cartel](/wiki/Rinnrivin_Di%27s_cartel "Rinnrivin Di's cartel") to achieve this. Seven years prior to the "[Napkin Bombing](/wiki/Napkin_Bombing "Napkin Bombing")" at the [New Republic senatorial complex](/wiki/New_Republic_senatorial_complex "New Republic senatorial complex") on [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime"), the First Order used the Amaxines to inject billions of [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") as start-up capital into Rinnrivin's cartel, turning the hitherto minor cartel into a major crime syndicate. Establishing a mutual relationship with the Amaxines, Rinnrivin embarked on lucrative smuggling and gambling operations with the proceeds being channeled through shadowy corporations and [Centrist](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists") sources back to the First Order, which used the money to rebuild its fleet. In addition, the Order also recruited several Centrist senators like [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Carise Sindian](/wiki/Carise_Sindian "Carise Sindian") as clandestine agents who worked to subvert the Republic from within. Many Centrists, an informal faction who were the rivals to the [Populists](/wiki/Populists "Populists") in the [New Republic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate"), and who favored a greater central government and military, admired the Old Empire's leaders and practices. Another proxy of the First Order was [Arliz Hadrassian](/wiki/Arliz_Hadrassian "Arliz Hadrassian"), a former [TIE fighter pilot](/wiki/Imperial_Starfighter_Pilot "Imperial Starfighter Pilot") who had become the leader of the Amaxine warriors. While Hadrassian saw the Amaxines as the vanguard of the First Order, Lady Carise regarded her as too volatile to manage. Hadrassian in return was impatient with the Centrists for refusing to secede from the Republic.[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51)

The First Order's operations were almost exposed when Rinnrivin Di's criminal activities began to exact a devastating toll on the planet [Ryloth](/wiki/Ryloth "Ryloth")'s off-world trade. In response, the New Republic senators [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") and [Ransolm Casterfo](/wiki/Ransolm_Casterfo "Ransolm Casterfo") embarked on an investigation which uncovered Rinnrivin's links to the Amaxine warriors. However, the two senators failed to discover the Order's linkages to the Amaxines and Rinnrivin's cartel. In an attempt to sow chaos, Arliz Hadrassian bombed the New Republic's senatorial complex. This set in motion a chain of events that led to the death of Rinnrivin and the destruction of most of the Amaxine warriors' forces on the planet [Sibensko](/wiki/Sibensko "Sibensko"). Hadrassian killed herself after [assassinating](/wiki/Tai-Lin_Garr%27s_assassination "Tai-Lin Garr's assassination") the Republic senator [Tai-Lin Garr](/wiki/Tai-Lin_Garr "Tai-Lin Garr"). While most Republic senators and the media believed that the demise of Rinnrivin's cartel and the Amaxines eliminated all threats to the Republic, Senator Organa disagreed with the New Republic's complacency. However, she was sidelined from the political process following a political scandal that led to the public revelation that her father was Darth Vader, which discredited Organa and forced her to resign from the Senate.[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51)

 [![The First Order claimed legitimacy as a successor state of the former Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/Legitimate_Power.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211205050001) [![The First Order claimed legitimacy as a successor state of the former Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/Legitimate_Power.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20211205050001)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/Legitimate_Power.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211205050001) 

The First Order claimed legitimacy as a successor state of the former Galactic Empire.

 

After the assassination of Tai-Lin Garr, Lady Carise and her Centrist counterparts began preparing a [motion to secede](/wiki/First_Order_secession "First Order secession") from the New Republic in order to join and support the First Order.[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51) Acting as a political coalition of worlds advocating centralized authority,[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) star systems aligned with the Centrists—including the planets [Arkanis](/wiki/Arkanis "Arkanis"), [Orinda](/wiki/Orinda "Orinda"), and [Kuat](/wiki/Kuat "Kuat")[[35]](#cite_note-Rise_and_Fall-35)—formally withdrew from the New Republic and joined the First Order[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) in [29 ABY](/wiki/29_ABY "29 ABY"),[[16]](#cite_note-BSI_note-16) marking the official formation of the First Order as a regime and beginning the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") between the First Order and the New Republic.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) While some in the Galactic Senate applauded the notion, others realized that without New Republic supervision, the former Imperials would return to the draconian ways of their predecessors.[[14]](#cite_note-Propaganda-14) Supreme Leader Snoke initiated a vast rearmament program, which would go on to produce a technologically superior military over the one that once existed under the Galactic Empire, and began subverting the Republic, as the First Order was keenly aware that it lacked the superior numbers and support of the former Imperial state.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27)

#### Preparations for war[]

##### Entering the scene[]

:   "*Through the ages, I've seen evil take many forms. The Sith. The Empire. Today, it is the First Order. Their shadows spreading across the galaxy. We must face them. Fight them. All of us..*"  
    "*There is no fighting against the First Order. Not one we can win.*"
:   ―Maz Kanata and Finn[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![The forces of the First Order emerged from the Unknown Regions, revealing the results of its rearmament program in defiance of the Galactic Concordance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/Might_is_All.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131043547) [![The forces of the First Order emerged from the Unknown Regions, revealing the results of its rearmament program in defiance of the Galactic Concordance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/Might_is_All.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180131043547)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/32/Might_is_All.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131043547) 

The forces of the First Order emerged from the Unknown Regions, revealing the results of its rearmament program in defiance of the Galactic Concordance.

 

The Centrist worlds that seceded from the New Republic provided the First Order with a foothold in the known galaxy,[[14]](#cite_note-Propaganda-14) by which time its military forces emerged from the Unknown Regions, precipitating the return of [fascism](/wiki/Fascism "Fascism") and militarism.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) In defiance of the Galactic Concordance, First Order forces frequently crossed the [Borderlands](/wiki/Borderlands "Borderlands"), launching several incursions into both Republic space and other [sectors](/wiki/Sector "Sector").[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43)[[53]](#cite_note-Cobalt_Squadron-53) The term "cold war" was used because there was no direct, large-scale fighting, but instead occasional minor skirmishes. Despite mounting First Order aggression, the New Republic refused to take forceful military action against the Order, seeking to avoid provoking another devastating galactic war at all costs.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) Meanwhile, the First Order utilized its political supporters and puppets within the Galactic Senate to ensure that the wider galaxy continued to consider them harmless, which also served to begin turning public opinion against those that opposed the Imperial successor.[[54]](#cite_note-Poe_17-54)

During this time, the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"), an offshoot of the [New Republic Defense Force](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Force "New Republic Defense Force"), was founded by General Leia Organa, who realized that the Senate could not protect the New Republic, alongside her few remaining allies, like [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar"), [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO"), [Joph Seastriker](/wiki/Joph_Seastriker "Joph Seastriker"), and [Temmin Wexley](/wiki/Temmin_Wexley "Temmin Wexley"). The Resistance acted as a check on the military designs of the First Order.[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51) General Organa released the [Grace Report](/wiki/Grace_Report "Grace Report") to the New Republic Senate, which publicly claimed that the Order was building hidden shipyards, armories, research-and-development labs, and academies, detailing the fact that facilities were working day and night on the massive military buildup.[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43) Meanwhile, the First Order began to expand and took over [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") with ease.[[55]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_-_Rose-55) During their career as a mercenaries that offered their services to unprotected star systems, [Zulay Ulor](/wiki/Zulay_Ulor "Zulay Ulor") and [Caracara Squadron](/wiki/Caracara_Squadron "Caracara Squadron") were brought into conflict with the First Order, which chased the starfighter squadron from restricted zones.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

In [33 ABY](/wiki/33_ABY "33 ABY"),[[15]](#cite_note-Timelines-15) Kylo Ren [led First Order forces against](/wiki/Battle_against_the_Benathy_(First_Order) "Battle against the Benathy (First Order)") the [expanding](/wiki/Benathy_expansion "Benathy expansion") [Benathy kingdom](/wiki/Benathy_kingdom "Benathy kingdom") and—following his victory over the [Benathy](/wiki/Benathy "Benathy")'s "[god](/wiki/Deity "Deity")," a [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Unidentified_Zillo_Beast_(Benathy) "Unidentified Zillo Beast (Benathy)")—declared the Benathy subjects of the First Order, which he ordered the Benathy to worship.[[56]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-56) By 34 [ABY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"),[[15]](#cite_note-Timelines-15) the First Order—having driven the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") [crime lady](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Harra](/wiki/Harra "Harra") from [her stronghold](/wiki/Harra_the_Hutt%27s_stronghold "Harra the Hutt's stronghold") on the [swamp](/wiki/Swamp "Swamp") planet [Vodran](/wiki/Vodran "Vodran")—proceeded to utilize the fortress as a [detention center](/wiki/Prison "Prison") that was overseen by [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Wanten](/wiki/Wanten "Wanten"), who was assigned as punishment for having allowed the building's previous owner to escape.[[46]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Vodran-46)

##### New Republic "relations"[]

:   "*The First Order is a remnant born of a war thirty years gone. Yes, they persist, yes, they continue, but by all accounts they do so barely. They are, at best, an ill-organized, poorly equipped, and badly funded group of loyalists who use propaganda and fear to inflate their strength and their importance.*"  
    "*They're flying state-of-the-art TIEs, they're using commando boarding parties and latest-generation attack shuttles in clear violation of the Galactic Concordance. They're training troops and pilots. We interrupted a military operation, Lonno, not some snatch and grab. They wanted the Yissira Zyde and they got it. They wanted it badly enough they paid for it with eight TIEs, those pilots, and however many people were aboard the shuttle that Muran and Iolo shot down. That's not a poorly organized force. That's not a poorly motivated force. That's a real threat.*"
:   ―Major Lonno Deso and Poe Dameron, after the Suraz engagement[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)

 [![The New Republic did not consider the First Order a threat to the galaxy, despite its military buildup.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/HuxAndStormtroopersAtCommandCenter-TFAOfficialTeaser.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150418182535) [![The New Republic did not consider the First Order a threat to the galaxy, despite its military buildup.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/HuxAndStormtroopersAtCommandCenter-TFAOfficialTeaser.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150418182535)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/HuxAndStormtroopersAtCommandCenter-TFAOfficialTeaser.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150418182535) 

The New Republic did not consider the First Order a threat to the galaxy, despite its military buildup.

 

Even as the First Order expanded its sphere of influence,[[57]](#cite_note-ResistanceAge-57) the New Republic Senate believed that the First Order posed no real, credible threat to the galaxy at large and the hard-won galactic peace. Echoing these sentiments, Chancellor [Lanever Villecham](/wiki/Lanever_Villecham "Lanever Villecham") argued there was no need for concern as long as the Order adhered to the dictates of the Galactic Concordance. Despite this, the First Order blatantly defied the accords by ushering in the mass mobilization of superior [stormtrooper](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper") forces, along with violating Republic bans on the sale of weapons to the First Order. Testing the resolve of the New Republic, small skirmishes occasionally erupted between the First Order and Republic, all while the Starkiller operation sought a suitable planet for implementation.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

With the First Order's growing threat and rapid mobilization for war, prominent members of the Republic voiced concern over the First Order, with the most vocal being former Senator Leia Organa.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) However, Organa—holding a reputation that was already damaged thanks to the revelations about her parentage[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51)—was largely scoffed at by the Senate at large as an alarmist and warmonger. Nonetheless, Organa used her influence as a prominent member of the former Rebel Alliance to recruit many former military officers who had been left forgotten by the [Military Disarmament Act](/wiki/Military_Disarmament_Act "Military Disarmament Act") passed by the Galactic Senate. Funded by like-minded senators who shared Organa's fears about the First Order, the Resistance came to serve as the opposing force to the Order's growing power, sparking a new phase of the continued Cold War.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

 [![The Resistance was formed as a result of the New Republic's unwillingness to risk open war with the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/OR-Kappa-2722_skirmish.png/revision/latest?cb=20160501201509) [![The Resistance was formed as a result of the New Republic's unwillingness to risk open war with the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/OR-Kappa-2722_skirmish.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160501201509)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/OR-Kappa-2722_skirmish.png/revision/latest?cb=20160501201509) 

The Resistance was formed as a result of the New Republic's unwillingness to risk open war with the First Order.

 

Meanwhile, the Republic Senate had become mired in corruption, darkness,[[57]](#cite_note-ResistanceAge-57) and bureaucracy,[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) amplified by the political gridlock caused by the divide between the Populists and the Centrists.[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51) Some Centrist politicians,[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) including senators like [Erudo Ro-Kiintor](/wiki/Erudo_Ro-Kiintor "Erudo Ro-Kiintor"), also colluded with the First Order for promises of wealth and power[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) or out of a legitimate belief in what they saw as the values of fascistic governance.[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51)[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) Large sums of credits were discreetly transferred to Ro-Kiintor through the [Corporate Sector Authority](/wiki/Corporate_Sector_Authority "Corporate Sector Authority"). Thanks to the work of such politicians[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) and a general fear in the Senate of wanting to avoid a new war,[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) the Resistance was forced to work on its own until it could obtain irrefutable evidence of First Order violations of the peace that could be presented to [New Republic Command](/wiki/New_Republic_High_Command "New Republic High Command"). During [Operation: Sabre Strike](/wiki/Operation:_Sabre_Strike "Operation: Sabre Strike"), [Resistance pilot](/wiki/Resistance_pilot "Resistance pilot") [Poe Dameron](/wiki/Poe_Dameron "Poe Dameron") and General Organa discovered that Senator Erudo had been colluding with the First Order and that he had valuable information about [Lor San Tekka](/wiki/Lor_San_Tekka "Lor San Tekka"), whom Organa believed could lead them to her brother, Luke Skywalker, who had gone into self-exile.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)

##### Annexation of the *Colossus*[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Occupation of the Colossus](/wiki/Occupation_of_the_Colossus "Occupation of the Colossus")

 [![The First Order deployed stormtroopers to the Colossus, ostensibly to protect the station from piracy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/HuntForKel-TheChildrenFromTehar.png/revision/latest?cb=20241028000129) [![The First Order deployed stormtroopers to the Colossus, ostensibly to protect the station from piracy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/HuntForKel-TheChildrenFromTehar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241028000129)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/HuntForKel-TheChildrenFromTehar.png/revision/latest?cb=20241028000129) 

The First Order deployed stormtroopers to the *Colossus*, ostensibly to protect the station from piracy.

 

The First Order began an [occupation of the *Colossus*](/wiki/Occupation_of_the_Colossus "Occupation of the Colossus") refueling station on the planet [Castilon](/wiki/Castilon "Castilon") as part of their preparations for their planned war against the rest of the galaxy. The First Order occupied the *[Colossus](/wiki/Colossus "Colossus")* under the guise of [peacekeepers](/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency "Law enforcement agency") in wake of several [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") raids on the platform, which the Order itself had secretly manufactured as a pretext of intervention so that the *Colossus* could be used as a staging ground.[[59]](#cite_note-The_New_Trooper-59)

The First Order had prior interest on the station; it had [placed](/wiki/Hunt_for_Eila_and_Kel "Hunt for Eila and Kel") a large [bounty](/wiki/Bounty "Bounty") of twenty thousand credits on [Kel](/wiki/Kel "Kel") and [Eila](/wiki/Eila "Eila"), which the Order claimed were members of a high-ranking First Order family from outside its military hierarchy. In actuality, Kel and Eila were orphaned survivors of the First Order's aggressive [actions](/wiki/Attack_on_Tehar "Attack on Tehar") against the people on [Tehar](/wiki/Tehar "Tehar").[[11]](#cite_note-The_Children_from_Tehar-11)

The First Order's presence was welcomed by some civilians on the *Colossus*, but others opposed the Order's measures, leading to a riot among the [alien](/wiki/Alien "Alien") population.[[59]](#cite_note-The_New_Trooper-59) In response, the First Order targeted residents who opposed or defied their control and placed them under arrest to be sent offworld under the pretext of an interest in security.[[60]](#cite_note-The_Disappeared-60)

#### The search for the last Jedi[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Hunt for Lor San Tekka](/wiki/Hunt_for_Lor_San_Tekka "Hunt for Lor San Tekka")

:   "*The droid will soon be delivered to the Resistance… leading them to the last Jedi. If Skywalker returns… the new Jedi will rise.*"
:   ―Snoke[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![Captain Phasma ordered Agent Terex to track the Resistance pilot Poe Dameron.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/TerexPhasma-PoeDameron2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190714012059) [![Captain Phasma ordered Agent Terex to track the Resistance pilot Poe Dameron.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/TerexPhasma-PoeDameron2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190714012059)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/TerexPhasma-PoeDameron2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190714012059) 

Captain Phasma ordered Agent Terex to track the Resistance pilot Poe Dameron.

 

In response to the Resistance's Operation: Sabre Strike, Captain Phasma dispatched Agent Terex to recover the information that Poe Dameron obtained from Senator Erudo. Terex's First Order strike force pursued Dameron and his [Black Squadron](/wiki/Black_Squadron_(First_Order) "Black Squadron (First Order)") to the planet [Ovanis](/wiki/Ovanis "Ovanis").[[17]](#cite_note-Poe_2-17) With the help of the unwilling spy, [Oddy Muva](/wiki/Oddy_Muva "Oddy Muva"),[[61]](#cite_note-Poe_11-61) Terex planted a tracker on Dameron's [T-70 X-wing starfighter](/wiki/T-70_X-wing_starfighter "T-70 X-wing starfighter").[[62]](#cite_note-Poe_1-62) A [skirmish](/wiki/Mission_to_Ovanis "Mission to Ovanis") took place on the skies over Ovanis and the [Cave of the Crèche](/wiki/Cave_of_the_Cr%C3%A8che "Cave of the Crèche"), which was complicated by the presence of the [Crèche](/wiki/Cr%C3%A8che "Crèche") cult and the hatching of two [winged creatures](/wiki/Unidentified_Cr%C3%A8che_creature "Unidentified Crèche creature"). Ultimately, Terex and his landing force were defeated. The [Crèche elder](/wiki/Unidentified_Cr%C3%A8che_elder "Unidentified Crèche elder") gave the information on Lor San Tekka to Dameron. To avoid war between the First Order and the New Republic, Terex and his surviving men were allowed to leave on their [Maxima-A class heavy cruiser](/wiki/Maxima-A-class_heavy_cruiser "Maxima-A-class heavy cruiser").[[63]](#cite_note-Poe_3-63)

 [![The First Order and the Resistance sought to find Lor San Tekka, who possessed the key to finding Jedi Master Luke Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/BlackSquadronCreche-PoeDameron3.png/revision/latest?cb=20190105040806) [![The First Order and the Resistance sought to find Lor San Tekka, who possessed the key to finding Jedi Master Luke Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/BlackSquadronCreche-PoeDameron3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190105040806)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/BlackSquadronCreche-PoeDameron3.png/revision/latest?cb=20190105040806) 

The First Order and the Resistance sought to find Lor San Tekka, who possessed the key to finding Jedi Master Luke Skywalker.

 

Terex later obtained intelligence that Black Squadron were [traveling](/wiki/Mission_to_Megalox_Beta "Mission to Megalox Beta") to [Megalox](/wiki/Megalox "Megalox") [prison](/wiki/Prison "Prison") on the high-gravity world of [Megalox Beta](/wiki/Megalox_Beta "Megalox Beta"). Dameron traveled to the prison world to question the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") crime lord [Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi](/wiki/Grakkus_Jahibakti_Tingi "Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi") about his knowledge of San Tekka's whereabouts. Terex bribed [Warden](/wiki/Warden "Warden") [Luta](/wiki/Luta "Luta") into abandoning Black Squadron to the prison population. Though Grakkus had made a deal with Terex to disclose the information, Grakkus changed his mind and decided to sell the information to whoever got him out first.[[64]](#cite_note-Poe_4-64)

Incensed at Grakkus' double-cross, Terex hired the crime lords [Isin](/wiki/Isin "Isin"), [Kan Be](/wiki/Kan_Be "Kan Be"), and [Toren](/wiki/Toren "Toren") to use their gangs to storm [Grakkus' fortress](/wiki/Fortress_of_Grakkus_the_Hutt "Fortress of Grakkus the Hutt") and kill Black Squadron. He planned to interrogate Grakkus and then kill him.[[65]](#cite_note-Poe_5-65) Grakkus' plan was, however, foiled by Black Squadron's [astromech droids](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") including [BB-8](/wiki/BB-8 "BB-8"), who deactivated Megalox's gravity shield. While Black Squadron and Grakkus escaped, Terex and his mercenaries were pinned down by the high gravity. Terex managed to escape aboard the *[Carrion Spike](/wiki/Carrion_Spike "Carrion Spike")* and attacked the [Megalox space station](/wiki/Megalox_space_station "Megalox space station"), seeking to punish Luta for letting Black Squadron escape. His ship blasted several shuttles but was forced to retreat when Black Squadron turned around and inflicted considerable damage on the *Carrion Spike*. Captain Phasma summoned Terex back to First Order space to report for debriefing, but Terex instead chose to pursue his nemesis Dameron.[[66]](#cite_note-Poe_6-66)

 [![Dameron was helped by Suralinda Javos, a journalist investigating the First Order's clandestine activities.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/VictoriousOnPheryon-PoeDameron7.png/revision/latest?cb=20161114075207) [![Dameron was helped by Suralinda Javos, a journalist investigating the First Order's clandestine activities.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/VictoriousOnPheryon-PoeDameron7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161114075207)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/VictoriousOnPheryon-PoeDameron7.png/revision/latest?cb=20161114075207) 

Dameron was helped by Suralinda Javos, a journalist investigating the First Order's clandestine activities.

 

Later, the *[Galaxy Beacon](/wiki/Galaxy_Beacon "Galaxy Beacon")* [journalist](/wiki/Journalist "Journalist") and former New Republic Starfleet member [Suralinda Javos](/wiki/Suralinda_Javos "Suralinda Javos") discovered that the First Order was building military installations, shipyards, weapons research facilities, and "something bigger" in violation of the Galactic Concordance. She met with Dameron on the Inner Rim gas giant of [Pheryon](/wiki/Pheryon "Pheryon"), hoping to sell the information to the Resistance in order to boost her journalistic career. However, the First Order Security Bureau Agent [Weel](/wiki/Weel "Weel") and his stormtroopers captured Javos and Dameron. During interrogation, Javos managed to kill Weel and free Dameron. After escaping, Javos decided to join the Resistance.[[67]](#cite_note-Poe_7-67)

Instead of returning to First Order space, Terex traveled to the crime haven of [Kaddak](/wiki/Kaddak "Kaddak").[[68]](#cite_note-Poe_8-68) There, he retook control of the Ranc Gang,[[69]](#cite_note-Poe_9-69) which he had helped create after the Battle of Jakku.[[50]](#cite_note-Poe_10-50) Against Captain Phasma's orders, Terex decided to use his Ranc Gang to destroy Poe and the Resistance. His plan involved giving false intelligence on the First Order to the Resistance [droid spy](/wiki/Resistance_spy_droid_network "Resistance spy droid network") [N1-ZX](/wiki/N1-ZX "N1-ZX") and tracking Dameron back to the Resistance base. Terex wanted to destroy the Resistance once and for all to aid the First Order's conquest of the galaxy. Terex's plans were upended when Dameron realized the deception and led Terex's Ranc Gang fleet to a [remote desert planet](/wiki/Unidentified_desert_planet "Unidentified desert planet").[[61]](#cite_note-Poe_11-61)

In addition, Oddy decided to break Terex's leverage on him by rescuing his wife [Sowa Chuan](/wiki/Sowa_Chuan "Sowa Chuan") and several slaves from Terex's flagship, *Carrion Spike*. While Terex led a landing party in pursuit of Dameron and the droids, Black Squadron [assailed](/wiki/Battle_over_a_desert_planet "Battle over a desert planet") Terex's ship and armada of "[Uglies](/wiki/Ugly "Ugly")."[[70]](#cite_note-Poe_12-70) Oddy and most of the slaves managed to escape in [escape pods](/wiki/Escape_pod "Escape pod") while Black Squadron provided firing cover. Terex's landing party was also wiped out by N1-ZX, who had been reprogrammed with [Mister Bones](/wiki/Mister_Bones "Mister Bones")'s droid personality template. Terex also fought with Dameron and BB-8 but was disarmed following a struggle. The battle came to an end when First Order forces under [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Malarus](/wiki/Malarus "Malarus") arrived and wiped out Terex's Ranc Gang fleet and flagship *Carrion Spike*.[[71]](#cite_note-Poe_13-71)

 [![Dameron delivered Terex to Commander Malarus, who arrested the rogue agent for risking open war between the First Order and the Resistance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/TerexArrested-PoeDameron13.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190104065623) [![Dameron delivered Terex to Commander Malarus, who arrested the rogue agent for risking open war between the First Order and the Resistance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/TerexArrested-PoeDameron13.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190104065623)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/TerexArrested-PoeDameron13.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190104065623) 

Dameron delivered Terex to Commander Malarus, who arrested the rogue agent for risking open war between the First Order and the Resistance.

 

Malarus had been dispatched by the First Order to arrest Terex, whose rogue mission violated Supreme Leader Snoke's directive to avoid open conflict with the New Republic and New Republic-aligned forces such as the Resistance. Malarus also led a landing party who met with Dameron and took the captive Terex into custody.[[71]](#cite_note-Poe_13-71) Malarus and Terex then went to [Abednedo](/wiki/Abednedo_(planet) "Abednedo (planet)") to capture Oddy Muva.[[54]](#cite_note-Poe_17-54) While onboard a transport, she had Terex interrogate Muva for information on the Resistance.[[72]](#cite_note-PD_18-72) Malarus however lost Muva with the aid of Dameron and Wexley, Malarus was then forced to watched as Muva made a suicide run on the *Enshado* and followed by her escape into hyperspace.[[73]](#cite_note-PD_19-73) Malarus then went to [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia") where she fought with Dameron.
