She was confronted by an official of [House Reya](/wiki/House_Reya "House Reya"), who arrested her and said they would give her a trial.[[74]](#cite_note-PD_23-74)

 [![Threatened by the return of the Jedi Order, the Supreme Leader prioritized the hunt for Luke Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Snoke_speaks_to_Kylo_Ren_and_Hux.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320231828) [![Threatened by the return of the Jedi Order, the Supreme Leader prioritized the hunt for Luke Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Snoke_speaks_to_Kylo_Ren_and_Hux.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160320231828)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/Snoke_speaks_to_Kylo_Ren_and_Hux.png/revision/latest?cb=20160320231828) 

Threatened by the return of the Jedi Order, the Supreme Leader prioritized the hunt for Luke Skywalker.

 

Seeking to locate a fragment of a [map](/wiki/Map_to_Skywalker "Map to Skywalker") that led to [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") Luke Skywalker[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)—who had gone into self-imposed exile following the failed resurrection of the Jedi Order, for which he blamed himself[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)—Supreme Leader Snoke believed that if Skywalker were to ever return, the new Jedi would rise, which would threaten the First Order's rise to power.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) As a result, the Supreme Leader deployed the Starkiller commanding triumvirate[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)—General Hux, Captain Phasma, and Kylo Ren—to Jakku, where Dameron and BB-8 had recovered the [star map](/wiki/Star_map "Star map") fragment from Lor San Tekka, an old ally of General Organa. Seeking to capture the droid, the First Order [assaulted](/wiki/Attack_on_Tuanul "Attack on Tuanul")[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) the [Church of the Force](/wiki/Church_of_the_Force "Church of the Force") settlement of [Tuanul](/wiki/Tuanul "Tuanul")[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) where San Tekka resided, but BB-8 was able to escape with the piece of the map.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![At Ren's command, First Order troops massacred a village on Jakku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/The_Massacre_at_Tuanul.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180201060612) [![At Ren's command, First Order troops massacred a village on Jakku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/The_Massacre_at_Tuanul.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180201060612)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/The_Massacre_at_Tuanul.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180201060612) 

At Ren's command, First Order troops massacred a village on Jakku.

 

The villagers of Tuanul fought back but were defeated; the survivors were then herded into a large group while San Tekka was brought to Ren himself, who demanded he turn over information on the map to the First Order. San Tekka claimed that Ren could not deny the truth that was his own family, causing Ren to slay the old man with his [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber"). Dameron then fired on Ren in retaliation, but the dark warrior [caught](/wiki/Force_Stasis "Force Stasis") the blast while his stormtroopers captured the pilot and brought him to[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) their [flagship](/wiki/Flagship "Flagship"), the [*Resurgent*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Resurgent-class_Star_Destroyer "Resurgent-class Star Destroyer") *[Finalizer](/wiki/Finalizer "Finalizer")*.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) Captain Phasma and her stormtroopers—except for [FN-2187](/wiki/Finn "Finn")—executed the remaining villagers on Ren's orders.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

FN-2187 and Dameron escaped the *Finalizer* aboard a stolen [TIE/sf space superiority fighter](/wiki/TIE/sf_space_superiority_fighter "TIE/sf space superiority fighter")[[75]](#cite_note-TFA_Cross-Sections-75) though not before Ren tortured Dameron and discovered the map fragment to be in a [BB-unit](/wiki/BB-series_astromech_droid "BB-series astromech droid") droid back on Jakku. During their escape, Dameron dubbed the renegade stormtrooper Finn. The pair crash landed in the [Goazon Badlands](/wiki/Goazon_Badlands "Goazon Badlands") on Jakku, where Finn presumed Dameron deceased. Finn eventually found BB-8 alongside a [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") named [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), but the First Order also found them, leading them to mark Rey as well and pursue the three across Jakku. However, Rey, Finn, and BB-8 were able to escape Jakku aboard the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*. They eventually stumbled on Rebellion war heroes and [smugglers](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca") in space, and the five of them traveled to [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana"), where they sought the help of [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata") in order to deliver BB-8 and the map fragment to General Organa at the [Resistance base](/wiki/Resistance_base "Resistance base").[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

On the First Order's secret Starkiller Base, General Hux informed Supreme Leader Snoke that their [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") was ready and proposed using it on the New Republic in order to draw out the Resistance. Supreme Leader Snoke authorized the operation and dismissed Hux before he conferred with Kylo Ren, with whom he discussed an apparent awakening in the Force. The Supreme Leader then informed his dark apprentice that the droid had fallen into the hands of his father, Han Solo, before cutting his holographic transmission to Starkiller Base.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

### First Order-Resistance War[]

#### Starkiller unleashed[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War")

:   "*Today is the end of the Republic. The end of a regime that acquiesces to disorder. At this very moment, in a system far from here… the New Republic lies to the galaxy… while secretly supporting the treachery… of the loathsome Resistance. This fierce machine which you have built… upon which we stand… will bring an end to the Senate! To their cherished fleet! All remaining systems will bow to the First Order! And will remember this… as the last day of the Republic!*"
:   ―Armitage Hux[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![The New Republic was destroyed by Starkiller Base as a demonstration of the First Order's power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/DestructionoftheHosniansystem.png/revision/latest?cb=20181009053535) [![The New Republic was destroyed by Starkiller Base as a demonstration of the First Order's power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/DestructionoftheHosniansystem.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181009053535)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/DestructionoftheHosniansystem.png/revision/latest?cb=20181009053535) 

The New Republic was destroyed by Starkiller Base as a demonstration of the First Order's power.

 

On the very eve of the planned war, General Hux delivered[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) a passionate[[76]](#cite_note-TLJCollector-76) speech to the legions of stormtroopers under his command who assembled to witness the destructive firepower of the weapon. Hux declared that the day would mark the end of the New Republic and denounced the Republic for lying to the galaxy, claiming that the Republic secretly supported the Resistance.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

After proclaiming that the remaining systems would bow to the First Order, General Hux commanded that the weapon be fired, and massive beams of energy were fired across the galaxy[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) from [Ilum](/wiki/Ilum "Ilum")[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) towards the Hosnian system. When the beams arrived, the astronomical bodies of the system were [destroyed](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm"), including the galactic capital of Hosnian Prime, and with it, the New Republic Senate and a [portion](/wiki/New_Republic_Home_Fleet "New Republic Home Fleet") of its [Defense Fleet](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Fleet "New Republic Defense Fleet").[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![A division of First Order stormtroopers invaded Takodana to acquire the map to Luke Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/FinnChewbaccaSoloCaptured-TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20191124202128) [![A division of First Order stormtroopers invaded Takodana to acquire the map to Luke Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/FinnChewbaccaSoloCaptured-TFA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191124202128)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/27/FinnChewbaccaSoloCaptured-TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20191124202128) 

A division of First Order stormtroopers invaded Takodana to acquire the map to Luke Skywalker.

 

As the First Order rose to power through the [Starkiller crisis](/wiki/Starkiller_crisis "Starkiller crisis"), it continued the hunt for the map to Skywalker, seeking to prevent the rise of the new Jedi. Its forces swiftly laid [siege](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana "Battle of Takodana") to [Maz Kanata's castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle") on Takodana and leveled it. Rey fled into the forests surrounding the castle, but Ren deployed stormtroopers to the woods before heading into the woods himself, hunting Rey down and eventually finding and capturing her. He probed her mind with the Force and realized that she had seen the map. Ren then decided that he would not need the droid, believing that he could instead interrogate her to find out what she had seen. Ren was notified of a Resistance surprise attack by a stormtrooper officer, who requested more troops, but Ren instead ordered the First Order [division](/wiki/Kylo_Ren%27s_division "Kylo Ren's division") to pull out, claiming that they had what they came for. First Order troops then boarded their ships and withdrew, taking the unconscious Rey along with them.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![The Battle of Starkiller Base ended in the superweapon's destruction.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/StarkillerBaseDestroyed-TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20220314045615) [![The Battle of Starkiller Base ended in the superweapon's destruction.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/StarkillerBaseDestroyed-TFA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220314045615)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/StarkillerBaseDestroyed-TFA.png/revision/latest?cb=20220314045615) 

The Battle of Starkiller Base ended in the superweapon's destruction.

 

Aided by the deserter FN-2187 "Finn," Solo and Chewbacca infiltrated Starkiller Base to rescue Rey and disable the planetary shields, allowing a Resistance [strike](/wiki/Battle_of_Starkiller_Base "Battle of Starkiller Base") to destroy the planet-converted superweapon. With the First Order minutes away from destroying the Resistance base on [D'Qar](/wiki/D%27Qar "D'Qar"), the team achieved their objectives, although Solo died in the process while trying to reconcile with Ren, his [son](/wiki/Solo_family "Solo family") with Organa. Escaping the planet with seconds to spare, the First Order's sun-harvesting superweapon was destroyed by the [Resistance Starfighter Corps](/wiki/Resistance_Starfighter_Corps "Resistance Starfighter Corps"), forming a new star where the planet once was. Supreme Leader Snoke ordered General Hux to leave the planet and come to him with Kylo Ren in order to complete his training.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) As Starkiller blew up, the damaged *[Retribution](/wiki/Retribution "Retribution")* that was under the command of [Gideon Hask](/wiki/Gideon_Hask "Gideon Hask") pulled out of hyperspace, its [hyperdrive](/wiki/Hyperdrive "Hyperdrive") [destroyed](/wiki/Skirmish_on_the_Retribution "Skirmish on the Retribution") by Resistance agents [Iden Versio](/wiki/Iden_Versio "Iden Versio"), [Zay Versio](/wiki/Zay_Versio "Zay Versio"), and [Shriv Suurgav](/wiki/Shriv_Suurgav "Shriv Suurgav"), who were on a mission to learn more about the First Order's [Project Resurrection](/wiki/Project_Resurrection "Project Resurrection").[[13]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-13)

#### Chasing the Resistance[]

:   "*They can't get away, Supreme Leader. We have them tied on the end of a string.*"
:   ―Armitage Hux, to Snoke[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

The First Order fleet had in large numbers regrouped for the new galactic war after the fall of Starkiller. Phasma returned from [chasing down](/wiki/Hunt_for_Rivas "Hunt for Rivas") and dispatching the true culprit on [Luprora](/wiki/Luprora "Luprora") who she blamed for being behind the one who had turned off the shields at Starkiller Base. She named [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Sol Rivas](/wiki/Sol_Rivas "Sol Rivas") as the perpetrator to General Hux.[[77]](#cite_note-Captain_Phasma_4-77) The surviving [Starkiller aerial defense force](/wiki/Starkiller_aerial_defense_force "Starkiller aerial defense force") pilots, such as [Poldin LeHuse](/wiki/Poldin_LeHuse "Poldin LeHuse"), were re-integrated into the fleet. They expressed a desire for vengeance and to prove themselves after failing to save the superweapon.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)

 [![In spite of Starkiller Base's destruction, the First Order stood poised to conquer the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/Episode_VIII_Stormtroopers.png/revision/latest?cb=20180621211457) [![In spite of Starkiller Base's destruction, the First Order stood poised to conquer the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/Episode_VIII_Stormtroopers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180621211457)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/Episode_VIII_Stormtroopers.png/revision/latest?cb=20180621211457) 

In spite of Starkiller Base's destruction, the First Order stood poised to conquer the galaxy.

 

Despite the loss of Starkiller Base, the First Order still possessed a secure and intact chain of command and massive military strength in the form of hundreds of battle-cruisers and millions of troops, emerging from the shadows to seize control of the galaxy by force. Following the loss of the Galactic Senate and the Hosnian system, the New Republic lost its leadership and its entire home fleet, which, due to the Military Disarmament Act, had been the majority of the Republic military.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)

Because of this imbalance, the New Republic was virtually helpless as First Order fleets spread across the galaxy,[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) all while the galaxy at large remained unaware of the destruction of Starkiller Base.[[78]](#cite_note-Black_Spire-78) These events quickly led to the collapse of the New Republic's authority over the galaxy as individual planets and governments began looking to their own interests. Surviving senators dissolved the Republic's remaining [task forces](/wiki/Task_force "Task force") in an effort to protect their own [homeworlds](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld")[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) while other worlds capitulated to the First Order in order to avoid direct military confrontation.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) As a result, the galaxy, as a whole, became divided.[[79]](#cite_note-Poe29-79)

 [![The Colossus was home to a Resistance cell that the First Order hunted in the Outer Rim.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/ColossusHunt-TheEngineer.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200101021137) [![The Colossus was home to a Resistance cell that the First Order hunted in the Outer Rim.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/ColossusHunt-TheEngineer.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200101021137)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/ColossusHunt-TheEngineer.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200101021137) 

The *Colossus* was home to a Resistance cell that the First Order hunted in the Outer Rim.

 

The core Resistance group found itself greatly outmatched by the First Order,[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) though the First Order also had to contend with other [Resistance cells](/wiki/Resistance_cell "Resistance cell").[[80]](#cite_note-The_Escape-80) The First Order failed to prevent the loss of intelligence on the specifications of the [*Mandator IV*-class Siege Dreadnought](/wiki/Mandator_IV-class_Siege_Dreadnought "Mandator IV-class Siege Dreadnought"),[[13]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-13) and further lost its grip over the *Colossus*, which [escaped](/wiki/Battle_of_Castilon "Battle of Castilon") Castilon into space.[[81]](#cite_note-No_Escape_2-81) However, with the loss of the New Republic and its unofficial support of their forces, the Resistance only possessed a few military ships and a few hundred soldiers. This led General Leia Organa to order the complete evacuation of the Resistance base on D'Qar while a First Order fleet led by General Hux was on its way to destroy the Resistance once and for all.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

 [![General Hux received direct instructions from the Supreme Leader to annihilate the entire Resistance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/SnokeHoloHux-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190904015617) [![General Hux received direct instructions from the Supreme Leader to annihilate the entire Resistance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/SnokeHoloHux-TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190904015617)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/95/SnokeHoloHux-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190904015617) 

General Hux received direct instructions from the Supreme Leader to annihilate the entire Resistance.

 

Setting their sights on the Resistance base, Hux's forces arrived in [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_D%27Qar "Battle of D'Qar") and destroyed the base, but the Resistance was able to escape before the First Order could finish them off. Despite escaping, the Resistance's speedy evacuation had cost them the vast majority of their remaining fleet and left them as fugitives wandering in space. Meanwhile, Supreme Leader Snoke summoned his apprentice, Kylo Ren, to his throne room on the *[Supremacy](/wiki/Supremacy "Supremacy")*, the First Order flagship, and mocked him for his failure at Starkiller Base and his ambitions to emulate Darth Vader.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

The mobile [supertanker fuel depot](/wiki/Supertanker_fuel_depot "Supertanker fuel depot"), the *Colossus*, shortly arrived in the aftermath of the D'Qar evacuation and [tried](/wiki/Skirmish_over_D%27Qar "Skirmish over D'Qar") to retrieve coaxium from the wreckage of the *Fulminatrix*. Phasma [tasked](/wiki/Hunt_for_the_Colossus "Hunt for the Colossus") [Pyre](/wiki/Pyre "Pyre") and Agent [Tierny](/wiki/Tierny "Tierny") with recovering the station or destroying it if recovery proved impossible due to its strategic importance and sought to prevent them from gaining the fuel, however this effort failed and the Resistance was able to successfully recovers coaxium and flee. Pyre and Tierny vowed to hunt for the *Colossus*.[[82]](#cite_note-Salvage_Run-82) Soon afterwards, Nikto [engineer](/wiki/Engineer "Engineer") [Nenavakasa Nalor](/wiki/Nenavakasa_Nalor "Nenavakasa Nalor") was sent [sabotage](/wiki/Sabotage_of_the_Colossus "Sabotage of the Colossus") the platform. Posing as a stranded spacer, but was discovered as a First Order spy. Though Nena escaped, they were able to managed to undo her sabotage and escape First Order forces.[[83]](#cite_note-The_Engineer-83)

 [![The Resistance was pursued through hyperspace by a fleet of First Order warships, including Snoke's flagship, the Supremacy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/Supremacy_out_of_hyperspace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220424195105) [![The Resistance was pursued through hyperspace by a fleet of First Order warships, including Snoke's flagship, the Supremacy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/Supremacy_out_of_hyperspace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220424195105)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/Supremacy_out_of_hyperspace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20220424195105) 

The Resistance was pursued through hyperspace by a fleet of First Order warships, including Snoke's flagship, the *Supremacy*.

 

Using [hyperspace tracking](/wiki/Hyperspace_tracker "Hyperspace tracker"), a newly developed technology descended and finally perfected from the Empire's [Tarkin Initiative](/wiki/Tarkin_Initiative "Tarkin Initiative"), the First Order tracked the Resistance to the [Oetchi system](/wiki/Oetchi_system "Oetchi system"),[[84]](#cite_note-TLJ_JR-84) catching them completely off guard and destroying one of their cruisers instantly. Kylo Ren, leading a TIE squadron in his personal fighter, attacked the Resistance's [command ship](/wiki/Command_ship "Command ship") [*Raddus*](/wiki/Raddus_(MC85_Star_Cruiser) "Raddus (MC85 Star Cruiser)") and blew up its hangar bay, taking out all of the Resistance's remaining fighters before he set his sights on the ship's [bridge](/wiki/Bridge_(starship) "Bridge (starship)"), where his mother, General Leia Organa, was. Though Ren was ultimately unable to bring himself to fire, his wingmen had no such qualms and fired on the bridge, exposing it to the vacuum of space and killing the majority of the Resistance's leadership, including Admiral Gial Ackbar. Organa was able to use the Force to pull herself back aboard, but she was left incapacitated. The Resistance's chain of command fell onto [Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Amilyn Holdo](/wiki/Amilyn_Holdo "Amilyn Holdo"), who oversaw their outrunning of the First Order, but their [fuel](/wiki/Fuel "Fuel") supplies were dangerously low, and one by one their other ships were running dry and being destroyed by the *Supremacy*'s [turbolasers](/wiki/Turbolaser "Turbolaser").[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

Once the *Raddus* was almost out of fuel, the Resistance began to fragment as desertions dramatically increased as members saw the struggle against the First Order as a lost cause. Later, a full-blown mutiny occurred as two sides formed among the crew: those who wanted to escape and hide from the enemy, and those who wanted to fight. This mutiny, led by Poe Dameron, was put down by the recovered General Organa, and the Resistance attempted to slip down to the former Rebel world of Crait. However, due to the capture of the Resistance infiltration team on the *Supremacy*, the First Order learned of the plan when the team code breaker [DJ](/wiki/DJ "DJ") betrayed the Resistance for his freedom and payment. This led the *Supremacy* to fire on the unarmed and unarmored[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) [U-55 orbital loadlifters](/wiki/U-55_orbital_loadlifter "U-55 orbital loadlifter"),[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) destroying roughly half of them.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

 [![Ren killed Snoke and usurped his position as Supreme Leader of the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/ActOfBetrayal-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20200204020859) [![Ren killed Snoke and usurped his position as Supreme Leader of the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/ActOfBetrayal-SoH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200204020859)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/46/ActOfBetrayal-SoH.png/revision/latest?cb=20200204020859) 

Ren killed Snoke and usurped his position as Supreme Leader of the First Order.

 

Meanwhile, Kylo Ren brought Rey to Snoke's throne room onboard the *Supremacy*, but Snoke's short reign over the galaxy ended as Ren killed his master along with his guards, while in a desperate sacrificial gamble to save the Resistance, Vice Admiral Holdo aimed the *Raddus* at the *Supremacy* and entered lightspeed. As a result, the ship collided with the First Order flagship and cleaved it and several *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyers in half, saving the Resistance remnant and causing heavy damage to the First Order fleet.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

Ren seized the title of Supreme Leader after the demise of Snoke. Driven by his rejection of the past, Ren endeavored to build a new galactic order by destroying the combined legacy of the Jedi, the Sith, the Rebellion, and all that came before. The First Order's forces quickly recovered, and, under the orders of the newly proclaimed Supreme Leader, sent an invading force of [All Terrain Armored Transport](/wiki/First_Order_All_Terrain_Armored_Transport "First Order All Terrain Armored Transport") and [All Terrain MegaCaliber Six](/wiki/All_Terrain_MegaCaliber_Six "All Terrain MegaCaliber Six") [walkers](/wiki/Walker "Walker") down to the [abandoned rebel base](/wiki/Crait_outpost "Crait outpost") on Crait where the Resistance was taking shelter.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) Ren personally led the siege of the Resistance's forces[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) at the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait").[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

 [![Luke Skywalker's sacrifice ensured the survival of the Resistance and the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/I-could-take-on-the-whole-empire-myself.png/revision/latest?cb=20211114201648) [![Luke Skywalker's sacrifice ensured the survival of the Resistance and the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/I-could-take-on-the-whole-empire-myself.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211114201648)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/I-could-take-on-the-whole-empire-myself.png/revision/latest?cb=20211114201648) 

Luke Skywalker's sacrifice ensured the survival of the Resistance and the Jedi Order.

 

During the battle, the *Millennium Falcon*, [piloted](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") by Chewbacca and Rey, arrived and attacked the First Order's TIE fighters, drawing them away from the battlefield. Even so, the battle led to the continued deaths of many of the remaining Resistance soldiers and personnel and the further depletion of its equipment. In addition, the Resistance's allies in the Outer Rim were called on for reinforcements, but did not arrive. However, Luke Skywalker unexpectedly appeared and confronted the First Order alone on the battlefield. Ren ordered all of the walkers to open fire on Skywalker in an attempt to destroy him. However, Skywalker miraculously emerged unscathed, and Ren went down to the surface to personally face his old Jedi Master. During their duel, Ren realized he was actually fighting a [Force projection](/wiki/Force_projection "Force projection") of Skywalker, who was still on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"). Skywalker's projection vanished, leaving Ren furious as the distraction bought time for the remaining few dozen Resistance personnel to flee aboard the *Millennium Falcon* with Rey's help.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

#### Long live the Supreme Leader[]

:   "*See what your enemies have done.* Snoke *is dead.* The Resistance *killed him. I am* Kylo Ren*. Your* Supreme Leader*. This is the end. This is the beginning. I will bring us to glory.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to the First Order[[85]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-85)

 [![A gathering of First Order stormtroopers looked upon the remains of Snoke before saluting his successor, Kylo Ren, as their new Supreme Leader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/SnokeCorpse-LegacyOfVader1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250207131713) [![A gathering of First Order stormtroopers looked upon the remains of Snoke before saluting his successor, Kylo Ren, as their new Supreme Leader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/SnokeCorpse-LegacyOfVader1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250207131713)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/SnokeCorpse-LegacyOfVader1.png/revision/latest?cb=20250207131713) 

A gathering of First Order stormtroopers looked upon the remains of Snoke before saluting his successor, Kylo Ren, as their new Supreme Leader.

 

Following the Battle of Crait, Kylo Ren returned to the First Order flagship, the *Finalizer*, where he introduced himself as the new Supreme Leader to an assembly of stormtroopers and officers, including General Hux, in the Star Destroyer's hangar. During his speech, Ren displayed the bisected corpse of Snoke to his troops and attributed his predecessor's death to the enemies of the First Order. After using the Force to cast Snoke's remains into the vacuum of space, Ren declared that his reign marked a new beginning for the First Order, which he would lead to glory. Ultimately, Ren's claim to power was accepted by the soldiers who collectively saluted their new leader.[[85]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-85)

After the speech, Ren summoned Hux to discuss the current state of the First Order, including Snoke' future plans and the resources at their disposal. Hux told Ren that, although the First Order still commanded the largest military in the galaxy, a large portion of their fleet was destroyed along with the *Supremacy*. In addition, the destruction of Starkiller Base deprived the First Order of its shipyard. When Hux offered to assemble a strike force to seize the resources they required, Ren ordered the general to instead focus on building a [throne](/wiki/Throne "Throne") that was worthy of the new Supreme Leader.[[85]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-85)

#### Conquering the galaxy[]

##### Across the stars[]

:   "*You control the galaxy's largest military, with the First Order, you could truly rule. You could fulfill the dream of so many of our forebears, rebuild the Empire.*"
:   ―Armitage Hux, to Kylo Ren[[85]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-85)

 [![The First Order took possession of vast swathes of the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/RedFury-GalaxysEdge4.png/revision/latest?cb=20190811060309) [![The First Order took possession of vast swathes of the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/RedFury-GalaxysEdge4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190811060309)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/RedFury-GalaxysEdge4.png/revision/latest?cb=20190811060309) 

The First Order took possession of vast swathes of the galaxy.

 

The new Supreme Leader set out to establish his dominion over the galaxy,[[86]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_5-86) with entire worlds surrendering in fear.[[83]](#cite_note-The_Engineer-83) The First Order had taken possession of the Outer Rim world of [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca") and even the Core World of [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia "Corellia") with little resistance as the galaxy having been left largely defenseless following the Starkiller incident. Stormtrooper forces raided the [hometown](/wiki/Pacer_Agoyo%27s_hometown "Pacer Agoyo's hometown") of [Pacer Agoyo](/wiki/Pacer_Agoyo "Pacer Agoyo"), injuring [his sister](/wiki/Puwanini "Puwanini") and burning down their house, which earned the First Order the hatred of Agoyo, who later joined the Resistance. An [emergency election on Akiva](/wiki/Emergency_election_on_Akiva "Emergency election on Akiva") resulted in the victory of a pro-First Order merchant while the First Order arrived on Ryloth, giving the Ryloth shipping guild five days to tithe before the shipping lanes would be [blockaded](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade"). The Resistance had fled to Ryloth, setting up in a [Ryloth Defense Authority base](/wiki/Ryloth_Defense_Authority_base "Ryloth Defense Authority base"), until a resident of [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City "Lessu City") betrayed them to the First Order. Despite a [First Order attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Ryloth "Attack on Ryloth") on the base, the Resistance escaped the planet.[[87]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-87)

At some point, the First Order had [annexed](/wiki/Annexation_of_Didyma_V "Annexation of Didyma V") the planet [Didyma V](/wiki/Didyma_V "Didyma V") and assumed control of its [lommite](/wiki/Lommite "Lommite") production, causing the [native](/wiki/Didynon "Didynon") [miner](/wiki/Miner "Miner") [Engi Golba](/wiki/Engi_Golba "Engi Golba") to flee his homeworld and join the Resistance, while the [Lumini pirates](/wiki/Lumini_pirates "Lumini pirates") were rendered defunct after an attack by the military junta left a young lieutenant named [Kuimi Enissa](/wiki/Kuimi_Enissa "Kuimi Enissa") as the sole surviving member.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) Meanwhile, as the First Order continued its march towards galactic conquest. Rebellious worlds[[88]](#cite_note-Parnadee_DB-88) such as [Kijimi](/wiki/Kijimi "Kijimi"), [Odynnia Gavo](/wiki/Odynnia_Gavo "Odynnia Gavo") and [Torost](/wiki/Torost "Torost") became contested locations that the First Order deployed its ground forces to under the command of General [Bellava Parnadee](/wiki/Bellava_Parnadee "Bellava Parnadee").[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

##### Resistance sightings[]

:   "*We can and will chase every rumor, every scrap, every vapor trail across the galaxy! We will mobilize every bounty hunter and informant and turn over every rock to find* all *of them…and wipe every one of them out of existence!*"
:   ―Kylo Ren, to Armitage Hux[[89]](#cite_note-Allegiance_1-89)

Sometime later, General Hux was informed of a sighting of Resistance operative Finn, but he dismissed it and told the lieutenant who had given him the information that the First Order wouldn't listen to every little word somebody said about the Resistance. Right then, Supreme Leader Ren came up to the bridge of the *Finalizer* and chastised Hux in front of the lieutenant, informing him that the First Order would in fact do anything to destroy the Resistance. To set an example, the First Order launched an assault that resulted in the [destruction](/wiki/Destruction_of_Tah%27Nuhna "Destruction of Tah'Nuhna") of the neutral world of [Tah'Nuhna](/wiki/Tah%27Nuhna "Tah'Nuhna") for assisting the Resistance after their escape from Crait.[[89]](#cite_note-Allegiance_1-89)

Meanwhile, [Mika Grey](/wiki/Mika_Grey "Mika Grey"), a traveler searching for [Sith artifacts](/wiki/Sith_artifact "Sith artifact") to keep them out of the First Order's hands, was being tracked by Agent [Raith](/wiki/Raith "Raith") and a squad of [First Order Raiders](/wiki/First_Order_Raider "First Order Raider"), stormtroopers commissioned by their commander, Supreme Leader Ren, with hunting down ancient Sith artifacts.[[90]](#cite_note-Raiders_DB-90) The Raiders were searching for a Sith [relic](/wiki/Unidentified_Sith_relic "Unidentified Sith relic") from a [buried temple](/wiki/Ashas_Ree_Sith_temple "Ashas Ree Sith temple") on [Ashas Ree](/wiki/Ashas_Ree "Ashas Ree"), where they [encountered](/wiki/Mission_to_Ashas_Ree "Mission to Ashas Ree") the *Colossus* Resistance cell and [Mika Grey](/wiki/Mika_Grey "Mika Grey"), a Force-sensitive [archaeologist](/wiki/Archaeologist "Archaeologist") who was also looking to acquire the relic. However, the First Order Raiders failed to acquire it and perished when the Sith relic unleashed an explosive wave of energy that incinerated Raith and his troops.[[91]](#cite_note-The_Relic_Raiders-91)

 [![Ren forbade the galaxy from having any contact with the Resistance on pain of death.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KyloRen-Allegiance2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623055027) [![Ren forbade the galaxy from having any contact with the Resistance on pain of death.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KyloRen-Allegiance2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210623055027)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KyloRen-Allegiance2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210623055027) 

Ren forbade the galaxy from having any contact with the Resistance on pain of death.

 

The First Order then went to neutral world of [Fondor](/wiki/Fondor "Fondor"), where a Resistance party had been spotted. A thorough, brutal interrogation of a Fondor [official](/wiki/Unidentified_human_male_(Fondor) "Unidentified human male (Fondor)") revealed that while the Resistance group went through the system, the official wouldn't lend any assistance. However, Supreme Leader Ren declared that even mere contact with the enemy was [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason"), and it gave him the excuse that he needed to put the [Fondor Shipyards](/wiki/Fondor_Shipyards "Fondor Shipyards") under complete First Order control. Ren then personally beheaded the official for this perceived treason with a swipe of his lightsaber—stating that the Empire had been too lenient.[[92]](#cite_note-Allegiance_2-92)

The First Order then prepared to make an example of [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala") after a fleet of at least twelve *Resurgent*-class warships arrived over Mon Cala acting on intelligence that the Resistance was there. There, a fleet of Mon Cala warships led by [Aftab Ackbar](/wiki/Aftab_Ackbar "Aftab Ackbar") managed to escape the planet's surface from the far side and jump to hyperspace, making the First Order aware that the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") and [Quarrens](/wiki/Quarren "Quarren") had chosen not to remain neutral and instead had given their support to the Resistance.[[93]](#cite_note-Allegiance_4-93) By then, the First Order had already had established a presence on Corellia.[[94]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Run-94)

##### Batuu and beyond[]

:   "*The First Order is on the verge of bringing unprecedented peace to the galaxy. An era of harmony once unimaginable amid the corruption and chaos of the New Republic.*"
:   ―A stormtrooper sergeant, 709th Legion[[86]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge_5-86)

 [![The First Order's invasion of the galaxy proceeded virtually unopposed following the annihilation of the New Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/RebuildingTheResistance-EpisodeGuide.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200120151834) [![The First Order's invasion of the galaxy proceeded virtually unopposed following the annihilation of the New Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/RebuildingTheResistance-EpisodeGuide.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200120151834)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/35/RebuildingTheResistance-EpisodeGuide.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200120151834) 

The First Order's invasion of the galaxy proceeded virtually unopposed following the annihilation of the New Republic.

 

As the war progressed, the First Order continued its manhunt for the surviving members of the Resistance, deploying forces to various locations across the galaxy,[[95]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge-95) while also dealing with cases of planetary and system rebellion.[[57]](#cite_note-ResistanceAge-57) Ren personally oversaw the search for Resistance fugitives at the [Black Spire Outpost](/wiki/Black_Spire_Outpost "Black Spire Outpost") on [Batuu](/wiki/Batuu "Batuu"), having traveled to the remote installation via a [TIE/es assault shuttle](/wiki/TIE/es_assault_shuttle "TIE/es assault shuttle") after receiving word that Rey had apparently been sighted on Batuu. Upon his arrival at [Docking Bay 9](/wiki/Docking_Bay_9_(Batuu) "Docking Bay 9 (Batuu)"), Ren was greeted by a First Order officer whom he deemed incompetent, and consequently strangled the officer by way of the Force.[[95]](#cite_note-Galaxy's_Edge-95) The First Order established [First Order Cargo](/wiki/First_Order_Cargo "First Order Cargo") to sell propaganda items to those passing through.[[96]](#cite_note-What_You_Need_to_Know-96)

First Order forces gained control of a [bacta](/wiki/Bacta "Bacta") production plant on [Tevel](/wiki/Tevel "Tevel"), but it was retaken by the Resistance and the [Tevellans](/wiki/Tevellan "Tevellan").[[97]](#cite_note-CYD-97) Sometime later, the First Order [light cruiser](/wiki/Light_cruiser "Light cruiser"), the *[Ladara Vex](/wiki/Ladara_Vex "Ladara Vex")*, was [dispatched](/wiki/Mission_to_Minfar "Mission to Minfar") to [Minfar](/wiki/Minfar "Minfar") in order to obtain a weapon that could control the [Zixon](/wiki/Zixon "Zixon") known as the [Echo Horn](/wiki/Echo_Horn "Echo Horn"), but it was destroyed by Resistance member sympathizers.[[98]](#cite_note-Spark_of_the_Resistance-98)

 [![Defeated by a Resistance cell, Agent Tierny suffered the price of failure when Supreme Leader Ren ended her life.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/NoMercyForTheWeak-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200128081835) [![Defeated by a Resistance cell, Agent Tierny suffered the price of failure when Supreme Leader Ren ended her life.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/NoMercyForTheWeak-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200128081835)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/NoMercyForTheWeak-TheEscape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200128081835) 

Defeated by a Resistance cell, Agent Tierny suffered the price of failure when Supreme Leader Ren ended her life.

 

The First Order seized control of the planet [Dantooine](/wiki/Dantooine "Dantooine"),[[99]](#cite_note-Rebuilding-99) which was once used as a [base](/wiki/Dantooine_base "Dantooine base") by the Rebel Alliance during the Galactic Civil War,[[100]](#cite_note-ANH-100) and established a [blockade](/wiki/Blockade_of_Dantooine "Blockade of Dantooine"), trapping a group of Resistance recruits on Dantooine until the arrival of the *Colossus* cell.[[99]](#cite_note-Rebuilding-99) As punishment for [Aeosian](/wiki/Aeosian "Aeosian") kingdom after it briefly hosted the *Colossus*, a First Order fleet was [dispatched to and bombarded](/wiki/Suppression_of_the_Aeos_system "Suppression of the Aeos system") the planet [Aeos Prime](/wiki/Aeos_Prime "Aeos Prime"). The attack proved to be too much for recent recruit [Tamara Ryvora](/wiki/Tamara_Ryvora "Tamara Ryvora"), who was rescued by the *Colossus* crew in a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Barabesh "Battle of Barabesh") that destroyed the Star Destroyer *[Thunderer](/wiki/Thunderer "Thunderer")*. Whereas Agent [Tierny](/wiki/Tierny "Tierny") was executed by Ren for their failings,[[80]](#cite_note-The_Escape-80) Commander Pyre went down with the ship.[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2)

#### A dark alliance[]

:   "*Forgive me, sir, but these allies on Exegol…they sound like a cult. Conjurers and soothsayers.*"  
    "*They've conjured legions of Star Destroyers. The Sith fleet will increase our resources ten-thousandfold. Such range and power will correct the error of Starkiller Base.*"
:   ―Domaric Quinn, to Kylo Ren, and Enric Pryde, to Domaric Quinn[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

In [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"),[[101]](#cite_note-TROS_Date-101) the Sith Eternal cult revealed itself to the galaxy by [broadcasting](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_broadcast "Palpatine's broadcast") a message that declared revenge using the voice of Emperor Palpatine, the widely known and public identity of the Dark Lord of the Sith, Darth Sidious, who was still believed to be dead. After this event, Supreme Leader Kylo Ren, who was determined to destroy any potential threats to his rule over the galaxy, diverted First Order resources to [search for the truth](/wiki/Search_for_Exegol "Search for Exegol"), resulting in him [finding](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(First_Order) "Mission to Mustafar (First Order)") a [Sith wayfinder](/wiki/Sith_wayfinder "Sith wayfinder") on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") [owned](/wiki/Vader%27s_wayfinder "Vader's wayfinder") by his grandfather, Darth Vader, which had been imbued by means of the Force with coordinates.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

 [![Ren was determined to destroy any potential threats to his rule and discover the truth of Darth Sidious return.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/IronwoodWarrior.png/revision/latest?cb=20210110044046) [![Ren was determined to destroy any potential threats to his rule and discover the truth of Darth Sidious return.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/IronwoodWarrior.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210110044046)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/40/IronwoodWarrior.png/revision/latest?cb=20210110044046) 

Ren was determined to destroy any potential threats to his rule and discover the truth of Darth Sidious return.

 

Ren utlized the [wayfinder](/wiki/Wayfinder "Wayfinder") to travel alone to his destination, where he discovered the hidden world of the Sith, Exegol, in the Unknown Regions. Within the [Sith Citadel](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel"), Sidious revealed himself to Ren and divulged that he had created the former Supreme Leader Snoke. Ren, unwilling to humor the phantom Emperor's attempts to intimidate him, readied himself to strike down Sidious. Before the killing blow could be delivered, Sidious revealed the culmination of his thirty-year [Contingency](/wiki/Contingency "Contingency"): the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) This massive fleet of planet-destroying [*Xyston*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Xyston-class_Star_Destroyer "Xyston-class Star Destroyer") had been created alongside an army of [Sith troopers](/wiki/Sith_trooper "Sith trooper") by the Sith Eternal cult, standing by on Exegol in preparation to wreak havoc upon the galaxy at large.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

After a generation, the work of the Emperor's followers was effectively complete;[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-4) the Sith Eternal military was on the verge of launching a full-scale invasion of the galaxy, its objective to restore Sith rule in the form of a new Sith Empire.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) The Emperor advised Ren that he could use the Sith fleet to succeed where his grandfather Vader failed, ruling the galaxy as the new Emperor. He offered Ren the fleet on the condition of killing the Jedi apprentice Rey. The Dark Lord then warned Ren that Rey was, in fact, his granddaughter, and thus a [Palpatine](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family") herself.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

 [![As part of a conspiracy decades in the making, the First Order was set to transformed into a resurgent Sith Empire with the Sith Eternal's fleet, the Final Order, on Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Unidentified_Star_Destroyer_fleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20190827043654) [![As part of a conspiracy decades in the making, the First Order was set to transformed into a resurgent Sith Empire with the Sith Eternal's fleet, the Final Order, on Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Unidentified_Star_Destroyer_fleet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190827043654)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Unidentified_Star_Destroyer_fleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20190827043654) 

As part of a conspiracy decades in the making, the First Order was set to transformed into a resurgent Sith Empire with the Sith Eternal's fleet, the Final Order, on Exegol.

 

At a meeting of the [Supreme Council](/wiki/First_Order_Supreme_Council "First Order Supreme Council") on the *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyer [*Steadfast*](/wiki/Steadfast_(Resurgent-class) "Steadfast (Resurgent-class)"),[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) Ren informed the [First Order officers](/wiki/First_Order_officer "First Order officer") that a spy in their ranks had supplied information to the Resistance. Though he was unaware of the mole's identity, Ren was confident that the fleet on Exegol would make him invincible, transforming the First Order into a true Empire. General [Domaric Quinn](/wiki/Domaric_Quinn "Domaric Quinn") expressed distrust over the Sith Eternal, denouncing them as a cult of conjurers and soothsayers. [Allegiant General](/wiki/Allegiant_General "Allegiant General") Enric Pryde countered that the Sith fleet would increase their resources ten thousandfold, correcting what he believed was the "error" of Starkiller Base. Ren [choked](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") General Quinn to death after he openly questioned the Supreme Leader as to what the Emperor was asking for in return. He then ordered the council to crush any worlds that defied them, and announced that he and his Knights of Ren were going hunting for "the scavenger," Rey.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

The First Order found Rey, alongside Finn, Dameron, and Chewbacca, on [Pasaana](/wiki/Pasaana "Pasaana") and alerted the local garrison. [First Order jet troopers](/wiki/First_Order_jet_trooper "First Order jet trooper") pursued them into the desert plains of Pasaana as the First Order arrived to Pasaana; the group escaped, though Chewbacca was captured by the Knights of Ren and brought on board Ren's Star Destroyer while Rey and Ren confronted each other in the desert. Later, the Knights of Ren tracked the group to [Kijimi](/wiki/Kijimi "Kijimi"), a world [occupied](/wiki/Occupation_of_Kijimi "Occupation of Kijimi") by the First Order.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

 [![Ren was determined to take the Emperor's throne with Rey, a Jedi apprentice, by his side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/DyadofKyloRenandRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200624095615) [![Ren was determined to take the Emperor's throne with Rey, a Jedi apprentice, by his side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/DyadofKyloRenandRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200624095615)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/DyadofKyloRenandRey-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200624095615) 

Ren was determined to take the Emperor's throne with Rey, a Jedi apprentice, by his side.

 

Ren arrived at Kijimi on his Star Destroyer and locked down the city. Finn and Poe Dameron were captured and, alongside Chewbacca, sentenced to execution, but Hux freed them, revealing himself to be the spy. The group liberated the *Millennium Falcon* and escaped, though not before Ren revealed to Rey that she was the granddaughter of Sidious and that they formed a [Force dyad](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad"). Pryde deduced Hux to be the spy and executed him on sight with a blaster rifle. Ren meanwhile conferred with Sidious over the Force; the Sith Lord threatened to turn his fleet against Ren if he betrayed their agreement, but Ren told Sidious he knew where Rey was going.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

#### Battle of Exegol[]

:   "*As I served you in the old wars, I serve you now.*"
:   ―Enric Pryde, to Darth Sidious — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/AsIServedYouInTheOldWars-TROS.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250402194243)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:AsIServedYouInTheOldWars-TROS.flac "File:AsIServedYouInTheOldWars-TROS.flac"))[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

 [![After Ren renounced the dark side, Sidious gave command of the Final Order fleet to Allegiant General Enric Pryde.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/SidiousOrdersPryde-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230129060904) [![After Ren renounced the dark side, Sidious gave command of the Final Order fleet to Allegiant General Enric Pryde.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/SidiousOrdersPryde-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230129060904)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/SidiousOrdersPryde-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230129060904) 

After Ren renounced the dark side, Sidious gave command of the Final Order fleet to Allegiant General Enric Pryde.

 

Ren confronted Rey alone among the [Death Star ruins](/wiki/Death_Star_ruins "Death Star ruins") on [Kef Bir](/wiki/Kef_Bir "Kef Bir"), an [ocean](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean") moon of [Endor](/wiki/Endor_(planet) "Endor (planet)"). The two fought in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel"); Ren bested Rey, but was distracted when his mother Organa reached out to him through the Force, allowing Rey to stab him with his own lightsaber before sensing Organa's presence. Rey healed her archenemy with the Force before leaving with his ship. Motivated by a memory of his late father, Han Solo, Ren renounced the dark side and reclaimed his identity as Ben Solo,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) abandoning the First Order in the process.[[102]](#cite_note-POV_213-102) Although Organa's sacrifice interfered with Sidious' plan, the Emperor was not deterred and instead refocused his efforts toward his granddaughter, Rey.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) With the Supreme Leader suddenly gone,[[102]](#cite_note-POV_213-102) Pryde became highest ranking member of the First Order,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) leaving him free to take his orders directly from the Emperor[[102]](#cite_note-POV_213-102) as he had in secret.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-4)

Pryde was contacted by Sidious while on board the *Steadfast*.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) The Imperial veteran,[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) having served the Emperor during the Galactic Civil War, pledged his allegiance and the First Order's to the Sith Lord,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) who in turn granted Pryde control over the Sith fleet, starting a unholy alliance with the Sith Eternal.[[103]](#cite_note-Sidious_BioGal28-103) With Pryde's support, Sidious decided that the time had come to deploy the Final Order throughout the galaxy. He summoned Pryde to Exegol and sent him a Sith Star Destroyer from the fleet,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) the *[Derriphan](/wiki/Derriphan "Derriphan")*,[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) to destroy Kijimi as a show of force against the Resistance. Following the [destruction of Kijimi](/wiki/Destruction_of_Kijimi "Destruction of Kijimi"), Pryde oversaw the fleet, which was in the process of departure when the Resistance arrived prior to the [Citizens' Fleet](/wiki/Citizens%27_Fleet "Citizens' Fleet"), resulting in the [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol").[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

 [![With the destruction of the Steadfast, the Sith fleet could not reinforce the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/SteadfastExegol-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200425153931) [![With the destruction of the Steadfast, the Sith fleet could not reinforce the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/SteadfastExegol-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200425153931)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/SteadfastExegol-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200425153931) 

With the destruction of the *Steadfast*, the Sith fleet could not reinforce the First Order.

 

During the battle, Pryde had the source of a navigation signal that the fleet needed to deploy off world switched from a [navigation tower](/wiki/Navigation_tower "Navigation tower") on Exegol to a beacon on his command ship. However, a Resistance [landing team](/wiki/Exegol_landing_team "Exegol landing team") made landing on Pryde's command ship. Former stormtroopers of [Company 77](/wiki/Company_77 "Company 77") covered Resistance troopers from their [orbaks](/wiki/Orbak "Orbak") as they fought against Sith troopers that landed to defend the ship. The landing team successfully knocked out the navigation tower and retreated, but the First Order personnel were able to reset it. At the same time Darth Sidious, after healing himself, attacked the Resistance and galactic forces, but he was stopped by Rey.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

She deflected Sidious' lightning back towards him, causing the Emperor to disintegrate and be destroyed at last, preventing the rebirth of the Sith. Meanwhile, former stormtroopers Finn and Jannah stayed behind on the hull of the ship and turned the ship's own turbolasers against it, killing Pryde and destroying the *Steadfast*, and with it, the navigation signal, preventing the remaining Sith Star Destroyers from launching off of Exegol and reinforcing the First Order. Finn and Jannah narrowly escaped aboard the *Millennium Falcon* with the help of General [Lando Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian") and Chewbacca as the *Steadfast* exploded and plunged to Exegol's surface.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7)

### Uprisings and the Downfall[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Uprising against the First Order](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order")

:   "*People are rising up all over the galaxy. Poe. We did it.*"  
    "*We did it.*"
:   ―Finn and Poe Dameron — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/PeopleAreRising-TheRiseOfSkywalker.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250402194337)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:PeopleAreRising-TheRiseOfSkywalker.flac "File:PeopleAreRising-TheRiseOfSkywalker.flac"))[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

 [![The Battle of Exegol was followed by a galaxy-wide uprising against the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Uprising_on_Cloud_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315163622) [![The Battle of Exegol was followed by a galaxy-wide uprising against the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Uprising_on_Cloud_City.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200315163622)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c1/Uprising_on_Cloud_City.png/revision/latest?cb=20200315163622) 

The Battle of Exegol was followed by a galaxy-wide uprising against the First Order.

 

In the aftermath of the Battle of Exegol, the First Order's forces came under attack by the populations that they had subjugated. Inspired by the victory of the Resistance and their rallied citizens' fleet, people [rose up](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order") all over the galaxy against the First Order, including on [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"), Endor, Jakku,[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) Coruscant, [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"), Corellia, [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal"), and [Thyferra](/wiki/Thyferra "Thyferra").[[104]](#cite_note-TROS_Junior_Novel-104) The First Order fell across the galaxy, and was ultimately defeated in the war.[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9)

### Legacy[]

:   "*The First Order bought death and tyranny with them out of the Unknown Regions.*"
:   ―Beaumont Kin, *The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire*[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58)

 [![Beaumont Kin following the end of the war said the First Order brought death and tyranny with them out of the Unknown Regions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/DB-Beaumont.png/revision/latest?cb=20240806023004) [![Beaumont Kin following the end of the war said the First Order brought death and tyranny with them out of the Unknown Regions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/DB-Beaumont.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240806023004)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/DB-Beaumont.png/revision/latest?cb=20240806023004) 

Beaumont Kin following the end of the war said the First Order brought death and tyranny with them out of the Unknown Regions.

 

With the war over, the galaxy's population began the long process of rebuilding as many First Order officers were captured and questioned by the Resistance in its immediate aftermath, which was recorded in the historian [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin")'s book, *[The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire](/wiki/The_Rise_and_Fall_of_the_Galactic_Empire "The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire")*, where he stated that the First Order bought death and tyranny with them out of the Unknown Regions. However, although Kin expressed satisfaction that the capture of numerous Imperial war criminals would see these individuals finally face justice for their atrocities, he also expressed his belief that the Resistance had a moral duty to help the countless young officers and stormtroopers that the First Order had raised inside its neo-Imperial doctrine from near-birth.[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58)

## Organization[]

### Government[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") and [First Order Supreme Council](/wiki/First_Order_Supreme_Council "First Order Supreme Council")

:   "*Our differences make us vulnerable. Vulnerable to misrule, corruption, to getting mired in bureaucracy instead of effecting real change. Stability ensures progress for everyone. That's the whole point of government.*"
:   ―Cardinal[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5)

 [![The Supreme Leader wielded absolute power and authority over the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/Supreme_Leader_Snoke_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20250215050936) [![The Supreme Leader wielded absolute power and authority over the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/Supreme_Leader_Snoke_TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250215050936)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/Supreme_Leader_Snoke_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20250215050936) 

The Supreme Leader wielded absolute power and authority over the First Order.

 

The Supreme Leader was a self-appointed position with absolute power over the First Order[[9]](#cite_note-TSWB-9) who delegated power to a number of high-ranking officers and [advisors](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor"), effectively removing any distinction between military and state. This formed an upper cadre of high-ranking officials, the [First Order High Command](/wiki/First_Order_High_Command "First Order High Command"), who had the authority to govern the First Order in the Supreme Leader's name. As Supreme Leader, Snoke was content to focus on spiritual matters, ceding control of military matters to generals and the shaping of the First Order's public image to [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda") masterminds. However, any and all alterations to the strategy required the Supreme Leader's approval, with personal interests regarded as secondary to orders from the Leader, while a "commanding triumvirate" of the First Order existed consisting of Kylo Ren, General Armitage Hux, and Captain Phasma, the leaders of [Starkiller Base](/wiki/Starkiller_Base "Starkiller Base").[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

Unbeknownst to even the highest echelons of the First Order, however, Snoke was in fact an artificial creation engineered by a hidden Sith cult, the Sith Eternal, under the directive of their master, Darth Sidious who returned from the dead, the Emperor of the Old Empire. Several addition clones of Snoke were stored on their hidden redoubt world, Exegol.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) Snoke served Darth Sidious and the Sith Eternal as a means to groom Ben Solo as Kylo Ren. Snoke kept his homeworld and origins concealed from the First Order so as to avoid revealing himself to be an artificial creation; nonetheless, some came to realize that Snoke was subservient to an unseen force and master.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

Due to the Supreme Leader's status in the First Order, an officer who had direct access to his person effectively wielded greater authority than their [military rank](/wiki/Military_rank "Military rank") would indicate.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) They oversaw the colonization of the Unknown Regions and destruction of the last Jedi. Much like Darth Vader in the former Empire, Kylo Ren existed outside the formal command structure of the First Order and frequently came into conflict with military officials owing to his agenda consistently trumping military objectives. Kylo's placement in the hierarchy not only maintained fear within the Order's upper ranks but also intentionally resembled that of Darth Vader's during the reign of the Old Empire.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) As a result, Ren was regarded as "the exception" to everything by his rival General Armitage Hux.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-4) It was the prerogative of the Supreme Leader to summon his subordinates at his pleasure, as well as to administer punishment to those who failed him.[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

 [![Supreme Leader would call conference to discuss goals for the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/PyreHuxConference-StationToStation.png/revision/latest?cb=20191225040413) [![Supreme Leader would call conference to discuss goals for the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/PyreHuxConference-StationToStation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191225040413)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/PyreHuxConference-StationToStation.png/revision/latest?cb=20191225040413) 

Supreme Leader would call conference to discuss goals for the First Order.

 

The Supreme Council was established under Supreme Leader Kylo Ren as an advisory board to replace the former triumvirate. It was formed by high-ranking members of High Command who served as [aides](/wiki/Aide "Aide") to Ren and had direct access to the highest levels of authority in the First Order, including the Supreme Leader. The council's purpose was to chart and implement the ongoing galactic conquest and plan the future of governing the galaxy. It was composed of Allegiant General Enric Pryde, Admiral [Frantis Griss](/wiki/Frantis_Griss "Frantis Griss"), Lieutenant [Draper](/wiki/Draper "Draper"), and Generals [Amret Engell](/wiki/Amret_Engell "Amret Engell"), Armitage Hux, [Bellava Parnadee](/wiki/Bellava_Parnadee "Bellava Parnadee"), and Domaric Quinn, allowing Ren to focus on spiritual matters as his predecessor had.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

Ren anticipated the council would be filled with infighting, to which he considered it good for his reign, as he preferred that they direct their energies against each other, thereby diminishing their chances of uniting against him.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

 [![The First Order lacked a traditional planetary capital, preferring mobile headquarters such as the Supremacy or the Steadfast.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/Supremacy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724161557) [![The First Order lacked a traditional planetary capital, preferring mobile headquarters such as the Supremacy or the Steadfast.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/Supremacy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220724161557)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/Supremacy.png/revision/latest?cb=20220724161557) 

The First Order lacked a traditional planetary capital, preferring mobile headquarters such as the *Supremacy* or the *Steadfast*.

 

Starkiller Base, a superweapon constructed within the planet Ilum,[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) hosted the largest military deployment in the First Order. However, it was not considered the official capital of the First Order because of Supreme Leader Snoke's policy of keeping the Order's headquarters mobile.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

Although various officers and allies of the First Order argued for a planet to act as their capital, Snoke rejected this idea and refused to designate capital command to a world either under direct First Order control or within the Unknown Regions, instead opting to command his underlings from his mobile command post, the [*Mega*-class Star Dreadnought](/wiki/Mega-class_Star_Dreadnought "Mega-class Star Dreadnought") *Supremacy*, making it the First Order's *de facto* capital.[[105]](#cite_note-TLJ:ICS-105)

### Military[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [First Order military](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military")

:   "*My men are exceptionally trained, programmed from birth.*"
:   ―Armitage Hux[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

 [![The Resurgent-class Star Destroyer was a successor to the Imperial-class Star Destroyer.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/TFA_FirstOrder_Star_Destroyer.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150604063321) [![The Resurgent-class Star Destroyer was a successor to the Imperial-class Star Destroyer.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/TFA_FirstOrder_Star_Destroyer.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150604063321)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/TFA_FirstOrder_Star_Destroyer.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150604063321) 

The *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyer was a successor to the *Imperial*-class Star Destroyer.

 

With its rapidly expanding military in clear violation of the Galactic Concordance and Republic laws, the massive militarization effort of the First Order continued throughout its tenure in the Unknown Regions. There, military bases and shipyards were constructed to churn out some of the technologically superior weapons and starfighters utilized by the Order's military. To avoid treaty restrictions banning the sale of weapons to the First Order, galactic arms manufacturers BlasTech Industries and Merr-Sonn Munitions, Inc. spun off a subsidiary known as the Sonn-Blas Corporation, which manufactured much of the First Order's weaponry within First Order space. [Sienar-Jaemus Fleet Systems](/wiki/Sienar-Jaemus_Fleet_Systems "Sienar-Jaemus Fleet Systems") also helped produce vessels such as the [*Upsilon*-class command shuttle](/wiki/Upsilon-class_command_shuttle "Upsilon-class command shuttle") and [TIE/fo space superiority fighter](/wiki/TIE/fo_space_superiority_fighter "TIE/fo space superiority fighter"), along with its two-seated variant the TIE/sf space superiority fighter.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

Additionally, Sienar-Jaemus Army Systems manufactured the widely used [Atmospheric Assault Landers](/wiki/AAL-1971/9.1_Troop_Transport "AAL-1971/9.1 Troop Transport") which could deploy twenty stormtroopers into the frontlines of combat, while the Aratech-Loratus Corporation developed the [LIUV](/wiki/Light_Infantry_Utility_Vehicle "Light Infantry Utility Vehicle");[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) When planetside, the First Order utilized a wide range of four-legged walkers similar to Imperial AT-ATs,[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) as well as the more advanced [All terrain Megacaliber Six](/wiki/All_Terrain_MegaCaliber_Six "All Terrain MegaCaliber Six"). In violation of New Republic laws regarding capital ships, [Kuat-Entralla Engineering](/wiki/Kuat-Entralla_Engineering "Kuat-Entralla Engineering") developed the *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyer, which featured more than 1,500 turbolasers, point-defense laser cannons and [ion cannons](/wiki/Ion_cannon "Ion cannon"), and was specifically designed to evoke the fearful image of the Old Empire's [*Imperial*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Imperial-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial-class Star Destroyer"). Though smaller than the [Imperial Navy](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy") at its height, the First Order Navy established itself as a formidable flotilla of destructive potential. Owing to the New Republic's disarmament efforts, the First Order armada swiftly conquered the galaxy virtually unchallenged.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

 [![Holding to the legacy of the Old Empire, the First Order trained a new generation of stormtroopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Star-wars-rise-of-the-resistance-hangar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210502195012) [![Holding to the legacy of the Old Empire, the First Order trained a new generation of stormtroopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Star-wars-rise-of-the-resistance-hangar.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210502195012)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Star-wars-rise-of-the-resistance-hangar.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210502195012) 

Holding to the legacy of the Old Empire, the First Order trained a new generation of stormtroopers.

 

Like its [predecessor](/wiki/Stormtrooper_Corps "Stormtrooper Corps"), the First Order Stormtrooper Corps was a component of the military that employed the use of stormtroopers,[[106]](#cite_note-TFA_Junior-106) including variants such as [snowtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_snowtrooper "First Order snowtrooper"). It also utilized specialists including [megablaster heavy assault troopers](/wiki/First_Order_heavy_trooper "First Order heavy trooper"), [flametroopers](/wiki/First_Order_flametrooper "First Order flametrooper"), and [riot control stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_riot_control_stormtrooper "First Order riot control stormtrooper") and selectively had one of the three variants placed in every ten-member stormtrooper squad. Unlike the inconsistent academy standards of the previous Galactic Empire, training of the new generation of stormtroopers emphasized improvisation and counter-insurgency operations, including guerrilla tactics. With the First Order lacking the numerical superiority of the Galactic Empire, better-equipped and -trained soldiers resulted in higher trooper proficiency than the previous Galactic Empire. Soldiers were often trained on capital ships and underwent vivid simulations to create the most loyal soldiers, which was an extension of the ideas of Commandant Brendol Hux and his [Commandant's Cadets](/wiki/Commandant%27s_Cadets "Commandant's Cadets").[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) It was strictly forbidden for a stormtrooper to initiate any contact with a officer in line with the First Order view on hierarchy.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27)

 [![Starkiller Base was a First Order superweapon capable of annihilating entire solar systems with a single blast.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/StarkillerResistance.png/revision/latest?cb=20220222201843) [![Starkiller Base was a First Order superweapon capable of annihilating entire solar systems with a single blast.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/StarkillerResistance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220222201843)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/StarkillerResistance.png/revision/latest?cb=20220222201843) 

Starkiller Base was a First Order superweapon capable of annihilating entire solar systems with a single blast.

 

One of its primary bases of operations was Starkiller Base, an [ice](/wiki/Water "Water") planet converted into a stronghold. Seeking to rule the galaxy through fear, the base housed a superweapon capable of destroying entire star systems by firing a planet-destroying beam through hyperspace, and was led by an unofficial triumvirate of General Armitage Hux, Kylo Ren, and Captain Phasma until it was destroyed in the Assault on Starkiller Base.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)[[107]](#cite_note-Starkiller_DB-107)[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

The scale of the First Order's military operation shocked complacent New Republic observers, who had believed such shows of force were merely part of local defense forces and ceremonial guards.[[14]](#cite_note-Propaganda-14) With the rapid expansion of the First Order's stormtrooper ranks and military capabilities, the Resistance believed that more trooper specializations were yet to be discovered, and ships even larger than the *Resurgent*-class Star Destroyers existed,[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) such as the *Mandator IV*-class Siege Dreadnought and the *Mega*-class Star Dreadnought.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) During both the Cold War and open conflict with the Resistance that followed, the First Order also employed its sympathizers for patrol and surveillance duties, utilizing older [Imperial *Gozanti*-class cruiser](/wiki/Imperial_Gozanti-class_cruiser "Imperial Gozanti-class cruiser") during such operations,[[108]](#cite_note-SWZ-108) while other collaborators made use of [*Raider*-class corvettes](/wiki/Raider-class_corvette "Raider-class corvette"), which remained a symbol of terror across the galaxy, even decades after the fall of the Galactic Empire that had first manufactured it.[[109]](#cite_note-Collaborators-109)
