 [![Technological development allowed the First Order to transform a planet into a superlaser platform.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425032958) [![Technological development allowed the First Order to transform a planet into a superlaser platform.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160425032958)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/Hux_and_Starkiller_Base.png/revision/latest?cb=20160425032958) 

Technological development allowed the First Order to transform a planet into a superlaser platform.

 

The First Order continued the research into dark energy translations and hyperspace tunneling that had began under the Old Empire, where they repurposed an ice world for the development of a mobile superweapon called Starkiller Base, which used a dark energy called "[quintessence](/wiki/Quintessence "Quintessence")" as it offered a virtual unlimited power source,[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) this was made possible after securing logs from secret Imperial laboratories detailing a suitable planet needed with the correct specifications for what would become Starkiller Base with the colossal superlaser array itself built into the planetary crust and would to the Order represent a technological step forward in power.[[110]](#cite_note-CL_2016-110)

 [![The Supremacy's hyperspace tracker technology was developed for military use.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/ShipboardTrackingControlComplex-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190503224609) [![The Supremacy's hyperspace tracker technology was developed for military use.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/ShipboardTrackingControlComplex-TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190503224609)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/61/ShipboardTrackingControlComplex-TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20190503224609) 

The *Supremacy*'s hyperspace tracker technology was developed for military use.

 

The First Order also developed the hyperspace tracker which was a type of [active tracker](/wiki/Active_tracker "Active tracker") with the ability to detect starships traveling through hyperspace developed by First Order scientists. Originally studied by the Tarkin Initiative during the reign of the Empire, the technology was not established for several more decades when a team assembled by General Armitage Hux discovered how to implement the technology. The hyperspace tracker utilized a complex [static hyperspace field generator](/wiki/Static_hyperspace_field_generator "Static hyperspace field generator"), which enveloped arrays of databanks and computers in a localized hyperspace field that accelerated their calculation speeds to unimaginable rates.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)

Additionally, the First Order constructed a [superlaser siege cannon](/wiki/Superlaser_siege_cannon "Superlaser siege cannon"), which was a form of miniaturized Death Star technology that was capable of firing a devastating energy pulse along a targeting tracer beam to cause a powerful detonation upon impact. Being a two-hundred-[meter](/wiki/Meter "Meter") cannon, it required support, such as having vehicles that were able to maneuver it into position during a siege and could be deployed to have a retractable stabilizing outrigger to ground its bulk.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) The First Order had also developed huge data banks loaded with centuries of combat reports and [astrogation](/wiki/Astrogation "Astrogation") data. This was aided by a static hyperspace field that accelerated their processing power to an unprecedented level, which was overseen by the [Shipboard Tracking Control Complex](/wiki/Shipboard_Tracking_Control_Complex "Shipboard Tracking Control Complex") that was the size of a planetary intelligence hub.[[105]](#cite_note-TLJ:ICS-105)

### Intelligence[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [First Order Security Bureau](/wiki/First_Order_Security_Bureau "First Order Security Bureau")

:   "*You're with the First Order now, Terex?*"  
    "*Yes, and it's* Agent *Terex. I'm an officer in their intelligence-gathering arm.*"
:   ―Kan Be and Terex[[65]](#cite_note-Poe_5-65)

 [![The First Order Security Bureau was the intelligence service of the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/FOSBAurebesh-Descent.png/revision/latest?cb=20190304140809) [![The First Order Security Bureau was the intelligence service of the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/FOSBAurebesh-Descent.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190304140809)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/50/FOSBAurebesh-Descent.png/revision/latest?cb=20190304140809) 

The First Order Security Bureau was the intelligence service of the First Order.

 

The First Order Security Bureau was the intelligence-gathering arm of the First Order, and was tasked with guarding state secrets and recovering information that had been stolen by the First Order's enemies.[[17]](#cite_note-Poe_2-17)[[67]](#cite_note-Poe_7-67)

Under Supreme Leader Snoke's directive, First Order agents and other First Order military forces were prohibited from seeking open hostility against forces aligned with the New Republic including the Resistance.[[61]](#cite_note-Poe_11-61)

### Outside affairs[]

#### Relationship with the New Republic[]

The First Order despised the New Republic as an illegitimate regime that tolerated disorder in the galaxy,[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) while the Republic did not officially recognize the First Order as a government,[[87]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-87) and instead viewed the Order as an ill-organized, poorly equipped, and badly funded group of Imperial loyalists.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) As a result, the Republic maintained an almost non-existent relationship with the First Order, resulting in ignored diplomatic protests and observers being denied access; an example of this was during the First Order [blockade](/wiki/Blockade_of_the_Otomok_system "Blockade of the Otomok system") of the [Otomok system](/wiki/Otomok_system "Otomok system"), to which the galactic government objected. However, the First Order informed them that the matter was an internal affair, which the Republic accepted.[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43)

In an effort to subvert the New Republic, the First Order also channeled funds through shell and third-party corporations in the [Corporate Sector](/wiki/Corporate_Sector "Corporate Sector") to corrupt Republic [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") like Erudo Ro-Kiintor, who blocked motions advocating sanctions against the First Order and increasing support for the New Republic Defense Fleet.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) Consequently, the First Order's main military adversary was the Resistance, a private military organization founded by General Leia Organa in response to the Republic's unwillingness to take action against the Order.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) The First Order saw its primary mission as restoring order to a lawless galaxy and viewed the Republic and Resistance as obstacles to achieving these goals.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)

 [![Prior to the fall of the New Republic, the First Order used diplomacy as a means of expanding its influence to other worlds.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/SecretsAndHolograms-EpisodeGuide.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181203220000) [![Prior to the fall of the New Republic, the First Order used diplomacy as a means of expanding its influence to other worlds.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/SecretsAndHolograms-EpisodeGuide.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181203220000)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/SecretsAndHolograms-EpisodeGuide.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181203220000) 

Prior to the fall of the New Republic, the First Order used diplomacy as a means of expanding its influence to other worlds.

 

Even though the First Order itself did not see the New Republic as a legitimate government,[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) the regime was willing to exploit its rival government's laws when possible. For example, the First Order could find blackmail in the form of discovering violations of Republic laws and use that discovery to its advantage; if the body with which the First Order was negotiating was not willing to agree to its terms, the First Order might threaten to inform the New Republic of actions, such as sanction violations, that body was responsible for. Alternatively, the First Order could use that possible blackmail as a counter to any threat of revealing First Order coercion; if the party wanted to reveal the First Order's actions, the First Order possessed the knowledge to damage that other body's standing.[[111]](#cite_note-The_High_Tower-111)

#### Relationships with other bodies[]

 [![In the era before open warfare, the First Order would attempt to complete their objectives through diplomacy before military action.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Benathy-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926101827) [![In the era before open warfare, the First Order would attempt to complete their objectives through diplomacy before military action.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Benathy-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190926101827)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/72/Benathy-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926101827) 

In the era before open warfare, the First Order would attempt to complete their objectives through diplomacy before military action.

 

The First Order was also known to have dealings with other entities like the Corporate Sector Authority,[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) the [Guavian Death Gang](/wiki/Guavian_Death_Gang "Guavian Death Gang"),[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) [Sheh Soahi's pirates](/wiki/Sheh_Soahi%27s_pirates "Sheh Soahi's pirates"),[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43) and Benathy kingdom, which the First Order attempted negotiations with before outright annexing after a battle.[[56]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-56) The First Order also established an alliance with the Warbird pirate gang while also attempting to make inroads with the government of the *Colossus* refueling platform,[[112]](#cite_note-The_Doza_Dilemma-112) which they intended to use as a staging ground for their further operations.[[59]](#cite_note-The_New_Trooper-59) Puppeteering both ends of the pirate-*Colossus* conflict, the First Order funded Warbird gang and supported its raids on the *Colossus*, all while attempting to negotiate with the *Colossus* on the promise that a First Order security detail could prevent those same raids.[[112]](#cite_note-The_Doza_Dilemma-112)

Captain Doza, the governing figure of the *Colossus*, initially rejected these attempted inroads,[[111]](#cite_note-The_High_Tower-111) much to the frustration of the First Order.[[112]](#cite_note-The_Doza_Dilemma-112) In one meeting with Doza, Major Vonreg offered protection from the pirate raids and a supply of fuel, only for Doza to counter that Vonreg was effectively attempting to coerce him. While Doza threatened to report the meeting as an act of coercion, Vonreg threated to, in turn, report Doza's own underworld dealings to the New Republic, which violated New Republic trade sanctions.[[111]](#cite_note-The_High_Tower-111)

Meanwhile, among individuals that continued to harbor sympathies for the Imperial state, the First Order and its claims to being a legitimate successor to the Galactic Empire was a matter of dispute. Although some veterans from the Imperial Military—such as Captain [Edrison Peavey](/wiki/Edrison_Peavey "Edrison Peavey"), Captain [Yago](/wiki/Yago_(First_Order) "Yago (First Order)"),[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) and the former stormtrooper Terex[[17]](#cite_note-Poe_2-17)—saw the Order as being a continuation of the [stratocratic](/wiki/Stratocracy "Stratocracy") regime that such individuals proceeded to join,[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) it was known to the former [journalist](/wiki/Journalist "Journalist") [Suralinda Javos](/wiki/Suralinda_Javos "Suralinda Javos") that a significant number of other individuals, while they identified as being Imperial, harbored little affinity for the military junta that sought to reclaim the Empire's legacy, regarding the Order as an "upstart." Some who had come to disagree with the Empire—like the warlord [Teza Nasz](/wiki/Teza_Nasz "Teza Nasz")—even proceeded to oppose the First Order, joining the Resistance in its efforts to fight the neo-Imperial rule.[[87]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-87)

#### Relations as the ruling government[]

:   "*We have learned from the mistakes of the Empire—They were too* lenient*.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[92]](#cite_note-Allegiance_2-92)

It is requested that this article section [be expanded](/wiki/Special:EditPage/:First_Order "Special:EditPage/:First Order"). *Please improve it in any way that you see fit, and remove this notice once the article section is more complete.*

About thirty years after the Battle of Endor, the First Order launched a preemptive attack on the Hosnian system in order to destroy the Republic and force the wider galaxy into submission. Later, the First Order successfully destroyed the Resistance's base on D'Qar. However, the remaining Resistance forces were able to evacuate[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) and continue their fight against the First Order.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) Under Supreme Leader Snoke, the First Order military rapidly expanded into the galaxy to wrestle control of space,[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) taking full advantage of the destruction of the New Republic and the collapse of whatever remained of the government.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27)

The expansion effort was carried on under the rule of Supreme Leader Kylo Ren, who further led the Order as an incredibly aggressive, punishing body. To Ren, the First Order needed to evolve beyond even the policies of the Empire, which he described as being "too lenient." As such, even the once neutral Fondor shipyards were nationalized by the First Order. Mere contact with the Resistance was regarded as an act of treason worthy of such a revocation of tolerance.[[92]](#cite_note-Allegiance_2-92)

### Judiciary[]

:   "*Our goal is galactic peace through absolute order.*"
:   ―Pyre[[113]](#cite_note-Descent_(episode)-113)

 [![In the First Order, disloyalty was regularly punished with public executions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/FOExecutioner_-_DKStickerBook.png/revision/latest?cb=20240216004053) [![In the First Order, disloyalty was regularly punished with public executions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/FOExecutioner_-_DKStickerBook.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20240216004053)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/FOExecutioner_-_DKStickerBook.png/revision/latest?cb=20240216004053) 

In the First Order, disloyalty was regularly punished with public executions.

 

There was no line between the military and justice in the First Order, which had a merciless attitude towards treason among other things, where it dispensed [final justice](/wiki/Death_penalty "Death penalty") on anyone with even slight loyalty issues per [day](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day"); this was done as several public executions with the executioners coming from the ranks of the Stormtrooper Corps anonymously in rotations, with it being considered an effective method of stormtrooper training. Unlike most stormtrooper variants, they were not from a specialist unit, but were instead randomly picked among regular stormtroopers for that day depending on various assignments and their identity was left anonymous.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)

Assigned to keep order on worlds within First Order territory, a specialized variant of the standard stormtrooper were trained in riot-control tactics and given non-lethal equipment to suppress any disorder,[[114]](#cite_note-DB-114) as well as some lethal weapons, such as the [Sonn-Blas](/wiki/Sonn-Blas_Corporation "Sonn-Blas Corporation") [F-11D blaster rifle](/wiki/F-11D_blaster_rifle "F-11D blaster rifle"), in case situations spiraled out of control.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

The First Order also used [cybernetics](/wiki/Cybernetics "Cybernetics") as a form of punishment by turning someone into a cyborg to ensure loyalty, as was the case with rogue agent Terex.[[115]](#cite_note-PD14-115) The First Order would also dismiss any strike action and would send in stormtroopers to enforce and "restore order" as part of a law and order operation, and would simply kill any negotiators to resolve any strike.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)

The First Order made it illegal to even communicate with the Resistance and considered it an act of treason that would result in being executed,[[92]](#cite_note-Allegiance_2-92) and the act of speaking ill of the Supreme Leader was determined as a crime.[[87]](#cite_note-Resistance_Reborn-87)

## Society and culture[]

### Overview[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Neo-Imperialism](/wiki/Neo-Imperialism "Neo-Imperialism")

:   "*It is the task of the First Order to remove the disorder from our own existence, so that civilization may be returned to the stability that promotes progress. A stability that existed under the Empire, was reduced to anarchy by the Rebellion, was inherited in turn by the so-called Republic, and will be restored by us. Future historians will look upon this as the time when a strong hand brought the rule of law back to civilization.*"
:   ―Kylo Ren[[116]](#cite_note-TFAn-116)

 [![The First Order was a totalitarian fascist society located inside the Unknown Regions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/FirstOrder.png/revision/latest?cb=20150811001647) [![The First Order was a totalitarian fascist society located inside the Unknown Regions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/FirstOrder.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150811001647)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/FirstOrder.png/revision/latest?cb=20150811001647) 

The First Order was a totalitarian fascist society located inside the Unknown Regions.

 

Due to being in isolation[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) in the Unknown Regions,[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) citizens of the First Order believed in an Imperially-skewed version of galactic history[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) and adopted a radical fascist,[[117]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-117) neo-Imperialist-based political ideology. That ideology's values were based on a fanatical devotion to the totalitarian notions of "order," violent disdain for the New Republic and democracy,[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) and survival of the fittest.[[118]](#cite_note-Live-118) Under the guidance of Imperial veterans, along with approved literature, vids, and mandatory viewings of morale sessions twice a day for stormtrooper cadets, officers learned of their glorious past and how they had been robbed of it by terrorists and rebels, who later called themselves the New Republic.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

### Relationship with the "Old Empire"[]

 [![A cultural divide existed within the First Order between loyalists to the "Old Empire" and the younger generation of First Order recruits.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/ForceMajeureLeibovitz.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240926185131) [![A cultural divide existed within the First Order between loyalists to the "Old Empire" and the younger generation of First Order recruits.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/ForceMajeureLeibovitz.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240926185131)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d9/ForceMajeureLeibovitz.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240926185131) 

A cultural divide existed within the First Order between loyalists to the "Old Empire" and the younger generation of First Order recruits.

 

Despite the guiding hand of old-style Imperials in forming the First Order,[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) the First Order's relationship with the Old Empire was a controversial subject even within the government.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) A culture clash emerged within the government's ranks between those old Imperial loyalists and the younger generation, who were much more dismissive of the fallen Empire and, in particular, Emperor Palpatine for the failure of the old Imperial state. The younger generation effectively believed in a vision of the Empire without need for the emperor himself, which created problems when Palpatine re-emerged[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119) in 35 ABY.[[15]](#cite_note-Timelines-15) The fallen Galactic Empire, overall, had a strange place in First Order culture[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119) as it represented both a glorious past[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) and a failed institution that needed to be grown past.[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119)

The presence of old loyalists such as Allegiant General Enric Pryde[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119) and Agent Terex, who openly longed for an outright return of the Empire, was counteracted by the likes of Captain Phasma[[17]](#cite_note-Poe_2-17) and Kylo Ren, whose personal ideology of "letting the past die" spoke to the First Order's attitude to the empire that preceded it.[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119) General Domaric Quinn, despite his prior service in the Empire,[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) stood politically with the younger generation.[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119)

While many of the old hands among the First Order officer corps, those who had once served during the Imperial Era, believed the First Order would restore the Empire to power, younger generations believed differently. General Armitage Hux, although raised to admire the accomplishments of the former Empire, believed that the war with the Rebel Alliance had been lost because of the internal flaws that existed inside the Imperial state. As a result, Hux saw the First Order as a more refined and pure version of what the Empire sought to become, but never achieved.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27) Similarly, Phasma disagreed with Terex about his comparing the First Order to the Empire, claiming that the former was purer than the latter had ever been, having been put through the crucible and emerged stronger as a result.[[17]](#cite_note-Poe_2-17)

### Propaganda and moral[]

 [![The First Order depicted itself as a strong, powerful force that alone could hold back chaos and corruption.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Holding_Back_the_Chaos.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131051032) [![The First Order depicted itself as a strong, powerful force that alone could hold back chaos and corruption.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Holding_Back_the_Chaos.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180131051032)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Holding_Back_the_Chaos.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180131051032) 

The First Order depicted itself as a strong, powerful force that alone could hold back chaos and corruption.

 

Many within the First Order believed only they could have the power necessary to wrestle the galaxy from a path of chaos and corruption.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) While the New Republic's corruption and ineffectiveness was plain to see across the galaxy, from its citizens to the Resistance and the First Order,[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) the First Order claimed its fascist policies were the answer the galaxy needed[[117]](#cite_note-Follow_and_Lead-117) while, in secret, actively contributing to the Republic's decline through its agents in the Senate.[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) The New Republic's corruption was one of the First Order's most potent weapons, as they ensured their agenda met with no interference from the Senate. The First Order's citizens saw this as proof the Rebellion was built on false promises, and that rebels could only tear down a government, not build one.[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5) All the while, however, First Order officers were driven by ego[[120]](#cite_note-Poe_Dameron_28-120) and personal ambition,[[119]](#cite_note-Rise235-119) damaging the overall mission of the state in the name of their personal pride.[[120]](#cite_note-Poe_Dameron_28-120) A large number of individuals in the First Order were non-human aliens who were effectively second-class citizens. This was apparent in the First Order propaganda and labor policies.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)

Pre-recorded speeches often filled the airwaves, in which General Armitage Hux commented on instances of the Republic's depravity, including famines on [Ibaar](/wiki/Ibaar "Ibaar") and [Adarlon](/wiki/Adarlon "Adarlon"), the brutal suppression of the people of [Balamak](/wiki/Balamak "Balamak"), and unchecked alien advances throughout the Outer Rim. Following these reports were stories of First Order victories such as liberating labor camps on [Iktotch](/wiki/Iktotch "Iktotch") or winning a fleet battle in the [Bormea sector](/wiki/Bormea_sector "Bormea sector"). Despite these patriotic functions and rallies, the First Order heavily relied on the brutal suppression of dissent and unpatriotic activities. Riot control stormtroopers were specially trained to quash insurrection, with live-fire dispersal of protesters permitted. Industrial unrest such as the [Strike at Pressy's Tumble](/wiki/Strike_at_Pressy%27s_Tumble "Strike at Pressy's Tumble") were blamed on New Republic agents. According to the First Order, the Jedi were officially extinct, and it was forbidden to pronounce Kylo Ren's birth name by order of Supreme Leader Snoke.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) To boost morale, the First Order utilized a commemorative [rank insignia system](/wiki/Rank_insignia_of_the_First_Order "Rank insignia of the First Order"), issuing armbands bearing the names of famous units and heroes of the Galactic Civil War. Many in the military believed that despite being outnumbered by the New Republic Starfleet, their technological superiority was so complete that even their smaller navy stood virtually unchallenged.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

### Recruitment and indoctrination[]

 [![The First Order conscripted human children, and indoctrinated them with state propaganda, ensuring absolute loyalty and devotion to its cause.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/DeckNine-AORFinn1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190704071609) [![The First Order conscripted human children, and indoctrinated them with state propaganda, ensuring absolute loyalty and devotion to its cause.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/DeckNine-AORFinn1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190704071609)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/DeckNine-AORFinn1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190704071609) 

The First Order conscripted human children, and indoctrinated them with state propaganda, ensuring absolute loyalty and devotion to its cause.

 

The First Order had no qualms with inducting children into direct combat.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) The most infamous example of the latter was the stormtroopers of the First Order, which forcibly subjected any children of worlds conquered by the First Order to military training.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) Because the First Order trained its soldiers from childhood, several members had very high ranks despite their youth technically making them closer to junior officers, in contrast to the Empire's [Sub-Adult Group](/wiki/Sub-Adult_Group "Sub-Adult Group"), which promoted patriotism without subjecting its members to direct combat.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) The First Order also instilled its [pilots](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") and [gunners](/wiki/Gunner "Gunner") with a fanatical devotion to it, training them to prioritize victory over their own survival.[[121]](#cite_note-Ordnance_Tech-121)

However brutal, the First Order's recruitment methods were lauded by their personnel and even by some of their conscripts. Many of the children the First Order recruited came from poor, impoverished Outer Rim worlds, where lawlessness was rampant and the residents had few to no prospects in life. Due to these horrific conditions, many of the people happily surrendered their children to the First Order willingly, either hoping they would have a better life or simply desiring payment and/or one or more fewer mouths to feed. Some freelance recruiters for the First Order agreed these children were better off under the First Order than on their homeworlds; one bragged that Athulla was such a "nightmare" the First Order was doing its children a favor.[[13]](#cite_note-Battlefront_II-13) One of these impoverished children inducted into the First Order's ranks, from the desert world of Jakku, would rise to become a respected officer in the First Order: Captain Cardinal. Other orphan children were recruited by force against their will while others were outright kidnapped from their families.[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5)

 [![The Benathy submitted to the First Order after their god was slain by Kylo Ren.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KneelBeforeRen-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926183308) [![The Benathy submitted to the First Order after their god was slain by Kylo Ren.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KneelBeforeRen-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190926183308)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/KneelBeforeRen-AORKyloRen1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190926183308) 

The Benathy submitted to the First Order after their god was slain by Kylo Ren.

 

Once recruited, citizens and soldiers of the First Order were indoctrinated to have a strong sense of duty, loyalty, and obedience to the state, and taught to forgo their personal desires for the greater good of the First Order. To this end, recruits abandoned their previous lives and identities upon their induction into the First Order and submitted to being identified by a numerical code. Senior officers and distinguished members of the Stormtrooper Corps, such as Phasma and Cardinal, were not expected to do so. First Order citizens were educated to believe it had been the pursuit of individual selfishness and desires that led the Rebel Alliance to topple the Old Empire. They were also taught that the rebels were short-sighted terrorists who could not see the benefit of the Old Empire, and instead started a war that forced it to crack down on personal liberties in response.[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5) The Benathy were not only indoctrinated into First Order ideology but worshiped the totalitarian regime itself after the death of the Zillo Beast that they worshiped as their god.[[56]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-56)

Despite this doctrine, First Order military training heavily emphasized individual strength and improvisation, both physically and mentally. Training programs that were mandatory for all recruits beginning at a young age became progressively more severe as they grew to adulthood. The First Order, like the Empire before it, believed the strong naturally rose to power, while the weaker were left to serve their natural leaders.[[5]](#cite_note-Phasma-5) Sometime during one's life within the First Order, they took an oath, one in which both high-ranking members such as General Artimage Hux or soldiers such as the former FN-2187 were cited as recipients, and in the First Order, renouncing that oath made them seen as something worse than even a Resistance fighter.[[116]](#cite_note-TFAn-116)

## Economy[]

 [![Pillaging entire worlds filled the First Order's coffers with various currencies, including coins minted from precious metals.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/Peggats_and_aurei_and_zemids.png/revision/latest?cb=20180204094955) [![Pillaging entire worlds filled the First Order's coffers with various currencies, including coins minted from precious metals.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/Peggats_and_aurei_and_zemids.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180204094955)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4f/Peggats_and_aurei_and_zemids.png/revision/latest?cb=20180204094955) 

Pillaging entire worlds filled the First Order's coffers with various currencies, including coins minted from precious metals.

 

The First Order economy was tightly controlled, partly due to treaty restrictions that prevented major galactic corporations from selling arms to the First Order, owing to its Imperial origins. Nevertheless, they had dealings with the Aratech-Loratus Corporation, [Rebaxan Columni](/wiki/Rebaxan_Columni "Rebaxan Columni"), Sienar-Jaemus Fleet Systems, Kuat-Entralla Engineering, and Sonn-Blas Corporation—a subsidiary of the First Order military's major arms manufacturers, Merr-Sonn Munitions, Inc. and BlasTech Industries. The First Order plundered the worlds within its domain in order to fill its coffers with various currencies, particularly coins minted from precious metals, such as [aurei](/wiki/Aurei "Aurei"), [peggats](/wiki/Peggat "Peggat"), and [zemids](/wiki/Zemid "Zemid"), all of which had universal value as they could be melted down.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) The credit was also a recognized currency in the First Order economy,[[11]](#cite_note-The_Children_from_Tehar-11) although by then coinage made from valuable metals was considered preferable to electronic currencies, especially in an era of instability.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)

Having amassed a vast treasury through conquest and plunder,[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) the First Order used its profits to purchase weapons from war profiteers on [Cantonica](/wiki/Cantonica "Cantonica") in the Corporate Sector.[[122]](#cite_note-Cantonica_DB-122)[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) They also channeled large sums of money through shells and third-party corporations with help from the Corporate Sector Authority.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)

To avoid the terms of the Galactic Concordance which included the sale of weapons to the Order, arms manufacturers [BlasTech Industries](/wiki/BlasTech_Industries "BlasTech Industries") and [Merr-Sonn Munitions, Inc.](/wiki/Merr-Sonn_Munitions,_Inc. "Merr-Sonn Munitions, Inc.") opted to bypass these restrictions by forming a subsidiary known as the Sonn-Blas Corporation, which manufactured all weapons within First Order space, while [Sienar-Jaemus Army Systems](/wiki/Sienar-Jaemus_Army_Systems "Sienar-Jaemus Army Systems") and [Aratech-Loratus Corporation](/wiki/Aratech-Loratus_Corporation "Aratech-Loratus Corporation") would develop spacecraft and vehicles to the Order.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

## Infrastructure[]

 [![The First Order upheld a number of factories and mines.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/StationThetaBlackFar-StationThetaBlack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181210220602) [![The First Order upheld a number of factories and mines.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/StationThetaBlackFar-StationThetaBlack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20181210220602)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/StationThetaBlackFar-StationThetaBlack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20181210220602) 

The First Order upheld a number of factories and mines.

 

The airwaves infrastructure in the First Order was under full state oversight and had tight restrictions and censorship imposed on it, which were often filled with pre recorded speeches in line with military objectives, this was there-for used by the ruling junta to maintain its control of the masses by using propaganda.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52)[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) The First Order utilized a form of holographic technology that could show the user in full color and lacked any scan lines as part of its communications systems.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6)

The *Supremacy* communication complex was used to watch [HoloNet](/wiki/HoloNet "HoloNet") traffic throughout the galaxy, this was to help identify trends and weaknesses that the First Order could use to further their goals, it could also be used to dispatched orders to agents operating within both New Republic and independent space.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) The *Supremacy* also held industrial capabilities including research labs and factories onboard, this housed departments for conception, research and well-stocked raw materials reserves, eight durasteel foundries as well as an asteroid mining complex for harvesting raw materials directly from asteroid fields, as well as state-of-the-art production lines that could not be cut off from supply lines. It also had at least eight droid manufacturing facilities.[[105]](#cite_note-TLJ:ICS-105)

[Station Theta Black](/wiki/Station_Theta_Black "Station Theta Black") [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station") was used to [mine](/wiki/Mining "Mining") and process [dedlanite](/wiki/Dedlanite "Dedlanite") to make [blasters](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster") for the army.[[123]](#cite_note-STB-123)

## Astrography[]

### Unknown Regions and Centrist worlds[]

 [![First Order was located in the Unknown Regions.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Absolution-PoeDameron24.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200609101110) [![First Order was located in the Unknown Regions.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Absolution-PoeDameron24.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/330?cb=20200609101110)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f5/Absolution-PoeDameron24.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200609101110) 

First Order was located in the Unknown Regions.

 

The territory ruled over by the First Order was identified simply as "First Order Space."[[124]](#cite_note-Poe_24-124) Initially, the territory of the First Order was located in the large, unexplored Unknown Regions to the west of the Core. An area of space outside of the New Republic's supervision, it served as the First Order and its associates' refuge.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) The overall territory was known as First Order Space[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) with the emerging power having expanded across the vast swaths of space left untouched for millennia by galactic explorers,[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) including [Demir](/wiki/Demir "Demir").[[125]](#cite_note-AoR_Phasma-125) Numerous shipyards, bases, and research facilities were also built on newly explored star systems and colonized worlds as the Order slowly expanded and plotted its eventual return to the galaxy at large.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8) The First Order undertook a major offensive against several of these kingdoms to seize their worlds and resources to fuel their rise.[[27]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-27)[[46]](#cite_note-Escape_from_Vodran-46)[[53]](#cite_note-Cobalt_Squadron-53)

The First Order also expanded into the Outer Rim Territories[[2]](#cite_note-Battles-2) beyond 29 ABY,[[16]](#cite_note-BSI_note-16) through the claiming of a bloc of star systems that seceded from the New Republic[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) and more underhanded tactics.[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43) The Centrists, a political faction in the Galactic Senate,[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51) wanted a more centralized government than the one offered by the New Republic. As a result, the systems that identified with Centrist politics joined the First Order, marking its official formation as a galactic government.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) At the time when the Centrists called for secession, the planets that supported their political goals included [Arkanis](/wiki/Arkanis "Arkanis"), [Comra](/wiki/Comra "Comra"), Coruscant, [Daxam IV](/wiki/Daxam_IV "Daxam IV"), [Hevurion](/wiki/Hevurion "Hevurion"), [Kuat](/wiki/Kuat "Kuat"), [Orinda](/wiki/Orinda "Orinda"), and [Riosa](/wiki/Riosa "Riosa").[[51]](#cite_note-Bloodline-51)

### Borderlands and pre-war expansion[]

 [![The Trans-Hydian Borderlands served as a neutral zone between First Order Space and the New Republic during the Cold War.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/TransHydianBorderlans-SWBTCTG.png/revision/latest?cb=20211120041536) [![The Trans-Hydian Borderlands served as a neutral zone between First Order Space and the New Republic during the Cold War.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/TransHydianBorderlans-SWBTCTG.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211120041536)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e1/TransHydianBorderlans-SWBTCTG.png/revision/latest?cb=20211120041536) 

The Trans-Hydian Borderlands served as a neutral zone between First Order Space and the New Republic during the Cold War.

 

A narrow region of neutral systems known as the Trans-Hydian Borderlands existed between New Republic and First Order space as a result of the Cold War between the two galactic powers, with peace negotiations leading to its service as a formal buffer zone. Despite frequent First Order incursions into Republic space, the Galactic Senate did not wish to spark a conflict, and thus was limited to formal diplomatic protest.[[52]](#cite_note-BTA-52) First Order assets, including galactic arms-manufacturing corporations such as BlasTech Industries and Merr-Sonn Munitions, Inc.'s Sonn-Blas Corporation subsidiary, took root and operated from within the region to evade the arms-selling restrictions mandated by First Order–New Republic treaty.[[8]](#cite_note-TFA_Visual_Dictionary-8)

In 33 ABY,[[15]](#cite_note-Timelines-15) the First Order assumed control over the Benathy kingdom, which ruled over an area of Wild Space.[[56]](#cite_note-Age_of_Resistance_Kylo-56) The First Order also made efforts to expand into the [Cassander sector](/wiki/Cassander_sector "Cassander sector") within the borderland by covertly supporting [Sheh Soahi's pirates](/wiki/Sheh_Soahi%27s_pirates "Sheh Soahi's pirates"), only for Resistance personnel to oppose those efforts via an [anti-piracy campaign](/wiki/Missions_against_pirates_in_the_Cassander_sector "Missions against pirates in the Cassander sector").[[43]](#cite_note-Bomber_Command-43) In the immediate leadup to the First Order-Resistance War, a number of planets that were not yet part of the First Order government considered joining it in return from the security the First Order promised.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12)

### Conquest of the galaxy[]

:   "*The First Order will control all the major systems within weeks.*"
:   ―Rey[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10)

The First Order increased its territorial extent from the Unknown Regions[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) through galactic conquest after the New Republic[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) was scattered[[58]](#cite_note-Rise-58) and destroyed.[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) At the unveiling of Starkiller Base, General Armitage Hux had promised that every system in the galaxy would bow to their regime with the New Republic's demise.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) Indeed, Rey knew that the First Order would claim every one of the galaxy's major systems in a matter of weeks[[10]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-10) after the unveiling of Starkiller Base,[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-6) the subsequent destruction of which had not become public knowledge.[[78]](#cite_note-Black_Spire-78) Hux's words about a galaxy-scale surrender contained great truth[[76]](#cite_note-TLJCollector-76) as planets surrendered to the incoming First Order,[[12]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-12) yet the regime would need to deal with cases of rebellion from planets and whole star systems during its reign over the galaxy.[[57]](#cite_note-ResistanceAge-57)

With its conquest of the galaxy, the First Order's military presence extended to various inhabited worlds, including Bespin, Jakku, and Endor.[[7]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-7) Kijimi was also conquered and placed under military occupation. No longer required to observe treaties with a fallen government, the First Order deployed its stormtroopers across the galaxy, making the white-armored soldier a common sight once more.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1) By 35 ABY,[[126]](#cite_note-Didyma_V-126) the First Order had [annexed](/wiki/Annexation_of_Didyma_V "Annexation of Didyma V") the world of [Didyma V](/wiki/Didyma_V "Didyma V"), taking control of its [lommite](/wiki/Lommite "Lommite") production.[[1]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-1)

## Behind the scenes[]

:   "*That all came out of conversations about what would have happened if the Nazis all went to Argentina but then started working together again? What could be born of that? Could The First Order exist as a group that actually admired The Empire? Could the work of The Empire be seen as unfulfilled? And could Vader be a martyr? Could there be a need to see through what didn't get done?*"
:   ―J.J. Abrams[[127]](#cite_note-Abrams_First_Order-127)

The First Order was created for the [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015") film [*Star Wars*: Episode VII *The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens") and was developed through conversations amongst the production team. According to [J.J. Abrams](/wiki/J.J._Abrams "J.J. Abrams"), the film's director, the team wondered what would have happened if the [Nazis](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazism "wikipedia:Nazism") who went into hiding in [Argentina](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Argentina "wikipedia:Argentina") after [World War II](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II "wikipedia:World War II") started working together again. Abrams hinted that the First Order would therefore be a group that admired the Galactic Empire and felt that its work was unfulfilled.[[127]](#cite_note-Abrams_First_Order-127)

The First Order's exact nature during the development of the film was kept secret since the film's announcement. On [August 10](/wiki/August_10 "August 10"), 2015, the official *Star Wars* Twitter and GooglePlus accounts unveiled an image of the First Order congregating at Starkiller Base.[[128]](#cite_note-First_Order_first_look-128)

Costume designer [Michael Kaplan](/wiki/Michael_Kaplan "Michael Kaplan") said the First Order uniforms were designed to look severe, "very hard edge, very broad shoulders, very angular, geometric." He cited inspiration from French fashion designer [Thierry Mugler](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thierry_Mugler "wikipedia:Thierry Mugler").[[129]](#cite_note-129)

*[Star Wars: The Rebel Files](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rebel_Files "Star Wars: The Rebel Files")* states that the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") did not have any [spies](/wiki/Spy "Spy") within the First Order.[[130]](#cite_note-The_Rebel_Files-130) However, *[Poe Dameron: Flight Log](/wiki/Poe_Dameron:_Flight_Log "Poe Dameron: Flight Log")* previously established that the [Resistance spy droid network](/wiki/Resistance_spy_droid_network "Resistance spy droid network") did have spies, including [RA-7-D4](/wiki/RA-7-D4 "RA-7-D4"), within the First Order.[[131]](#cite_note-Flight_Log-131)

[↑](#cite_ref-Didyma_V_126-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* dates the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IX_The_Rise_of_Skywalker "Star Wars: Episode IX The Rise of Skywalker") to one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode VII *The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens"). As *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the events of *The Force Awakens* to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"), the events of *The Rise of Skywalker* must occur in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"). Since [Engi Golba](/wiki/Engi_Golba "Engi Golba") was a [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") member during the events of Episode IX, then [Didyma V](/wiki/Didyma_V "Didyma V") had already been annexed by that time. 127. ↑ [127.0](#cite_ref-Abrams_First_Order_127-0) [127.1](#cite_ref-Abrams_First_Order_127-1) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) [Kylo Ren Is Not A Sith](http://www.empireonline.com/news/story.asp?NID=45203) by Dyer, James on Empire Magazine ([August 25](/wiki/August_25 "August 25"), [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015")) ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20151018205158/http://www.empireonline.com/news/story.asp?NID=45203) archived on [October 18](/wiki/October_18 "October 18"), [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015")) 128. [↑](#cite_ref-129) [Premium-Era-real](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Premium-Era-real.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019125517) ['Star Wars' Costume Designer Breaks Down 'The Force Awakens'](http://ew.com/gallery/star-wars-force-awakens-costume-gallery/2418323_general-hux) by Smith, C.
